| `Board: Split Focused Pane Vertical` (`260715-6jwn`) | Only on `/board/<name>` and ‚â•1 pane | `executeSplit(focusedPane.server, .windowId, true, .cwd)` ‚Äî `splitWindow` with `horizontal: true`, mirroring the terminal *palette*'s Vertical‚Üí`horizontal:true` mapping (the documented top-bar-chip-vs-palette flag divergence, left out of scope). Keyboard parity for the board SplitButtons (Constitution V) |
| `Board: Split Focused Pane Horizontal` (`260715-6jwn`) | Only on `/board/<name>` and ‚â•1 pane | `executeSplit(focusedPane.server, .windowId, false, .cwd)` ‚Äî `horizontal: false`; mirror of Vertical |
| `Board: Kill Focused Pane` (`id: board-kill-focused`, `260718-co9z`; renamed from `board-close-focused` / "Board: Close Focused Pane") | Only on `/board/<name>` and ‚â•1 pane | `requestKillFocused` ‚Äî opens the **kill confirm dialog** (¬ß Board Kill Confirm Dialog) rather than firing immediately; confirmed Kill is a window-kill (`killWindow` ‚Üí `POST /api/windows/{id}/kill`) whose `onSettled` schedules `refetch()`. Keyboard parity for the board ‚úï (Constitution V) |
| `Board: Move up` / `Board: Move down` (`260708-a2qd`) | Only on `/board/<name>`, boundary-hidden (not first / not last) | Reorder the CURRENT board in the board list ‚Äî keyboard/touch parity for the board-list drag (Constitution V). Computes the full order via `computeMoveOrder` and POSTs `setBoardOrder`; see ¬ß Board-list drag reorder + ¬ß Command Palette Move up/down |
| `Board: Move Focused Pane Left` (`260708-rmiq`) | Only on `/board/<name>` when `focusedIndex > 0` (hidden at the left edge ‚Äî not disabled) | Moves the focused pane one slot left ‚Äî fires the same single `reorder(...)` POST as DnD, computing `before`/`after` via `computeMoveNeighbors` (¬ß Board Pane Reorder). No wraparound. Keyboard parity for the drag reorder (Constitution V) |
| `Board: Move Focused Pane Right` (`260708-rmiq`) | Only on `/board/<name>` when `focusedIndex < entries.length - 1` (hidden at the right edge) | Moves the focused pane one slot right ‚Äî mirror of Move Left |
| `Board: Toggle Autofit (on/off)` (`260708-738w`, `id: board-toggle-autofit`) | Only on `/board/<name>` (label reflects the current state) | Flips the per-board desktop autofit preference (same state the top-bar `BoardAutofitToggle` reflects ‚Äî Constitution V parity). Desktop layout only; a no-op on the mobile carousel. See ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle |

**v1 limits**: The right-click context menu pin entry is not implemented (use sidebar pin icon, command palette, or board pane header). Hover-to-focus is disabled in v1. *(The former "`Board: Reorder Pane` deferred to v1.1" limit is superseded by `260708-rmiq` ‚Äî DnD reorder + the Move Focused Pane Left/Right palette entries above ship the reorder capability. See ¬ß Board Pane Reorder.)*

The AppShell palette mount carries `Board: Switch to <name>` + the `Pin: Current Window to <board>` direct-pin set + `Pin: Current Window to new board‚Ä¶` + `Board: Unpin Current Window` (`260718-gxrq`; the inline `Board: Pin Current Window`/`board-pin-current` opener was removed ‚Äî superseded by the new-board variant). The BoardPage's own palette mount (`boardRouteActions` useMemo in `board-page.tsx`) carries `Switch to <name>` + `Leave Board View` + the boundary-hidden `Board: Move up/down` (`260708-a2qd`) + the entries-gated `Cycle Pane Focus ‚Üí/‚Üê` + `Unpin Focused Pane` (`260704-9o7k`) + the entries-gated `Board: Split Focused Pane Vertical/Horizontal` + `Board: Kill Focused Pane` (`260718-co9z`, renamed from `Board: Close Focused Pane`) + the boundary-gated `Move Focused Pane Left/Right` (`260708-rmiq`; Left pushed only when `focusedIndex > 0`, Right only when `focusedIndex < entries.length - 1`; the cycle/unpin/split/kill/move-pane entries all sit inside a single `entries.length > 0` guard) + the always-present `Board: Toggle Autofit (on/off)` (`260708-738w`, ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle ‚Äî parity for the top-bar `BoardAutofitToggle`, outside the `entries.length > 0` guard) ‚Äî board-route-only entries that AppShell's palette can't surface because the board route does not render AppShell. The split/kill/unpin actions all consume shared `board-page.tsx` handlers rather than re-deriving state (parsimony): the `focusedPane` memo (`entries[focusedIndex]` ‚Üí `{server, windowId, cwd}`, cwd from the active pane, hoisted above `boardRouteActions`) feeds the split executors (`executeSplit`, `useOptimisticAction`-wrapped `splitWindow` with `addToast` on error) and the kill opener `requestKillFocused` (which routes through the confirm dialog whose confirmed Kill runs `executeKillWindow` ‚Äî `killWindow` ‚Äî scheduling `refetch()` via `onSettled`, ¬ß Board Kill Confirm Dialog), and the shared `unpinFocused` callback backs both the palette unpin and (via the tile header) the header unpin ‚Äî **plus** the globally-meaningful actions duplicated in because the board mounts its own palette: the terminal-font trio (Increase / Decrease / Reset terminal font ‚Äî the board's panes are live terminals, ¬ß Terminal Font Size) followed by `View: Refresh Page` and `Help: Documentation`. The returned array composes as `[...switchEntries, ...conditional, ...fontEntries, refreshEntry, helpEntry]` (`refreshEntry` from `260703-p29w`, `helpEntry` from `260704-hmd0`). The board is the degraded-relay recovery scenario ‚Äî N live relay WebSockets ‚Äî and since `260704-9o7k` a top-bar RefreshButton also renders in board mode (L3 always-block), so the palette entry is now the keyboard-parity form rather than the board's *only* reload affordance. **Since `260713-4zap`** the return array also appends `...updateEntries` (`buildUpdateActions`, ¬ß Update Notification) LAST ‚Äî `[...switchEntries, ...conditional, ...fontEntries, refreshEntry, helpEntry, ...updateEntries]` ‚Äî following the same dual-mount duplication convention: below `sm` the top-bar UpdateChip is hidden, so the board palette is a phone user's only update surface on `/board/$name`.

### Pin palette actions (`Pin:` prefix, `260718-gxrq`)

`buildPinActions` (`app/frontend/src/lib/palette-pin.ts`) is the pure, dependency-free builder for the command-palette pin actions, following the `lib/palette-move.ts` / `lib/palette-version.ts` / `lib/palette-view.ts` convention (label composition, exclusion, and ordering are unit-testable without mounting the shell). Signature `buildPinActions(boards, alreadyPinned, lastUsed, onPin, onOpenNewBoardPopover): PaletteAction[]`:

- One **direct-pin** action per board the current window is NOT already pinned to ‚Äî `id: pin-current-<board>`, label `Pin: Current Window to <board>`, ordered last-used-first via `orderBoardsLastUsedFirst` (over the already-pinned-filtered set). `onSelect` ‚Üí `onPin(board)`.
- The **new-board variant** last ‚Äî `id: pin-current-new-board` (`PIN_NEW_BOARD_ACTION_ID`), label `Pin: Current Window to new board‚Ä¶`, `onSelect` ‚Üí `onOpenNewBoardPopover()`. Always present (the only free-text entry seam).
- Edge cases: window pinned to every board, or zero boards ‚Üí only the new-board variant.

**Wiring** (`app.tsx` `boardActions` useMemo): gated on `sessionName && currentWindow && server` (mirrors the removed inline action's gating) so the actions are available on the terminal/server route for the current window. `onPin` calls `usePinActions.pin(server, windowId, board)`; `onOpenNewBoardPopover` dispatches the existing `pin-popover:open` CustomEvent (`{ detail: { server, windowId } }`) that the matching `WindowRow` handles. `alreadyPinned` = `currentWindowPinnedBoards` (derived from the cross-board pin map); ordering uses `readLastPinnedBoard()`. The board-route palette mount (`board-page.tsx`) is unchanged. **Supersedes** the inline `board-pin-current` (`Board: Pin Current Window`) action, which is REMOVED ‚Äî its popover-opening role is the new-board variant, and the per-board entries add the direct keyboard pin that closes the Constitution V gap.

### Pin last-used preference (`lib/last-pinned-board.ts`, `260718-gxrq`)

Client-side "last board a window was pinned to" preference ‚Äî per-client only (Constitution II, no backend persistence), `runkit-*` key convention (`LAST_PINNED_BOARD_KEY = "runkit-last-pinned-board"`, alongside `runkit-terminal-font-size`, `runkit-update-dismissed`). Reads/writes are best-effort try/catch-noop (mirroring `lib/window-view.ts`) so private mode / quota / SSR never throw.

- `readLastPinnedBoard(): string | null` ‚Äî value NOT validated against the live boards list here; callers filter it (a board disappears when its last pin is removed).
- `writeLastPinnedBoard(name: string): void` ‚Äî called at the **single** pin site inside `usePinActions.pin` (see ¬ß Hooks (Frontend)) on every successful pin, so all entry points (popover, palette) keep the preference consistent.
- `orderBoardsLastUsedFirst(boards, lastUsed): BoardSummary[]` ‚Äî returns `boards` with a valid live last-used board moved to the front; a stale/absent `lastUsed` (board gone, or `null`) is ignored and input order preserved; the input array is never mutated (fresh array on reorder, same reference on no-op). Consumed by both the popover ordering and `buildPinActions`.

### Post-pin success feedback + toast optional action (`260718-gxrq`)

`usePinActions.pin` surfaces success feedback (before this it toasted only on error). On a successful pin it fires `addToast("Pinned to <board>", "info", { label: "View board", onSelect: () => navigate to /board/<board> })` ‚Äî placed in the hook (not per call site) so every pin entry point gets the same feedback; the hook runs inside router context so it obtains `useNavigate` directly. `unpin`/`reorder` stay error-only.

This required a minimal extension to the **toast system** (`components/toast.tsx`, see ¬ß Error toast system): `ToastEntry`/`addToast` gain an optional `action?: { label: string; onSelect: () => void }` as a **THIRD positional argument** ‚Äî `addToast(message, variant?, action?)`, NOT an options object ‚Äî which preserves all existing positional call sites with zero churn. The action renders as a keyboard-focusable `<button>` inside the toast body (the toast body is already `pointer-events-auto`); selecting it dismisses the toast then runs `onSelect`.

### Command Palette View actions (`View:` prefix)

`viewActions: PaletteAction[]` (`useMemo` in `app.tsx`) is the AppShell palette's `View:`-prefixed block, composed into `paletteActions` between `boardActions` and `terminalFontActions` (see ¬ß Boards Command Palette). Its static entries are:

| Entry | Visibility | Action |
|-------|------------|--------|
| `View: Text Input` | Only when `sessionName` is set (a terminal is in view) | Toggles the docked compose strip (`toggleComposeStrip`) ‚Äî palette parity for the `>_` chip (¬ß Docked Compose Strip) |
| `View: Terminal` / `View: Web` / `View: Chat` (`260714-t97o-web-view-lens`; chat `260714-r7rq`) | Each shown only when its lens is **available** (`availableViews(currentWindow)`, which folds in the `chatProvider` gate) **AND not the current** (`resolvedView`) view; `shortcut` hint = `` Ctrl+` `` for `View: Chat` (and `View: Terminal` when LEAVING chat), else `‚åò.` | `switchView(view)` ‚Äî the per-viewer lens switch (no `@rk_type` mutation). Built by the ONE pure `buildViewActions(available, resolved, onSwitch)` (`lib/palette-view.ts`); see ¬ß Window Views (Lens Model) ‚Üí Palette parity. **Replaced the retired `toggle-iframe-terminal`** action (which mutated `@rk_type`) AND the chat feature's separate `buildViewActions(chatAvailable, ‚Ä¶)` call |
| `View: Fixed Width (900px)` / `View: Full Width` | Always (label reflects `fixedWidth` state) | `toggleFixedWidth` |
| `View: Refresh Page` | Always (ungated) | `window.location.reload()` ‚Äî a full page reload (`260703-p29w-topbar-refresh-button`) |

**`refresh-page` is appended ungated after `toggle-fixed-width`** ‚Äî a full-page reload is meaningful on every AppShell route (tmux Server `/$server`, Terminal `/$server/$window`), unlike the terminal-only top-bar `RefreshButton` (¬ß Chrome (Top Bar)). It is the keyboard-reachable form of that recovery affordance (constitution V).

**Dual-mount duplication** ‚Äî because the app mounts **two** CommandPalettes (AppShell's, driven by `paletteActions`; and the board route's own, driven by `boardRouteActions`) and the board route does NOT render AppShell, a globally-meaningful action must be **registered in both** to be reachable everywhere. `refresh-page` follows the **terminal-font-trio precedent** (Increase/Decrease/Reset terminal font, ¬ß Terminal Font Size): both the trio and `refresh-page` live in `app.tsx`'s AppShell blocks AND are duplicated into `board-page.tsx`'s `boardRouteActions` (¬ß Boards Command Palette). This is intentional duplication, not a shared source ‚Äî the two palettes have disjoint mounts. The `run-kit: Update‚Ä¶`/`Dismiss Update Notice` actions (`260713-4zap`, ¬ß Update Notification) follow the SAME convention ‚Äî built by the shared pure `buildUpdateActions` helper (`lib/palette-update.ts`) and folded into BOTH `app.tsx`'s `updateActions` and `board-page.tsx`'s `boardRouteActions` ‚Äî with the extra motivation that below `sm` the top-bar UpdateChip is hidden, so the board palette is a phone user's only update surface. The **Host page (`/`) mounts NO CommandPalette** (pre-existing ‚Äî the Host-page `HostOverviewPage` has no palette), so `refresh-page` is unreachable there and that was scoped out (adding a Host-page palette mount would grow UI surface against constitution ¬ßIV). Nothing in the codebase claims broader reach than "every mounted palette" ‚Äî the reach comments at `app.tsx` `viewActions` and the `top-bar.tsx` `RefreshButton` docblock name the actual scope (AppShell palette + board palette; the Host page mounts none).

### Command Palette `PR: Refresh Status` action (`260715-jykd-manual-status-refresh`)

`PR: Refresh Status` is the keyboard-first parity (Constitution ¬ßV) for the PANE-header refresh button (¬ß Collapsible Panels ‚Üí WindowPanel). It triggers the same `refreshStatus()` ‚Üí `POST /api/status/refresh` best-effort kick of both PR pollers (fresh state via SSE).

It follows the established **pure-builder** convention (mirrors `lib/palette-view.ts` / `lib/palette-update.ts`): the label/id live in `buildStatusRefreshAction(onRefresh)` (`lib/palette-status-refresh.ts`, colocated `.test.ts`) ‚Äî a single `{ id: "status-refresh", label: "PR: Refresh Status", onSelect: onRefresh }` action whose body is the caller-supplied `onSelect`. `app.tsx` memoizes it as a `statusRefreshActions: PaletteAction[]` group (`buildStatusRefreshAction(() => void refreshStatus().catch(() => {}))`, empty deps ‚Äî the callback closes over the static import) and folds it into the AppShell `paletteActions` aggregation (between `configActions` and `updateActions`, in both the array spread and its dependency list). **AppShell-only** (not dual-mounted into `board-page.tsx`'s `boardRouteActions`) ‚Äî the refresh is server-global but the affordance is labeled around the PANE panel, which the board route does not render; the top-bar/PANE surfaces cover the board user. The label is `PR:`-prefixed (scope honesty ‚Äî it refreshes PR/status freshness, not "all pane stats"; the other PANE registers are already fresh within ~7.5s).

### Hooks (Frontend)

| Hook | File | Returns |
|------|------|---------|
| `useBoards()` | `hooks/use-boards.ts` | `{ boards, isLoading, error }`. Initial `listBoards()` on mount; subscribes to `board-changed` SSE on every server returned by `listServers()` (boards are server-scoped since `260602-qn62`, but the board LIST is summarized across servers, so it attaches all to catch each one's pin/unpin/reorder events); 50ms debounce coalesces rapid events; preserves last good value on transient error |
| `useBoardEntries(name)` | `hooks/use-boards.ts` | `{ entries, isLoading, error, refetch }`. Initial `getBoard(name)`; subscribes on all known servers (the board list spans servers, so a pin/unpin on any server may affect this board); same debounce + error tolerance. `refetch` (= `fetchEntries`, added `260715-6jwn`) forces a re-fetch bypassing the SSE debounce ‚Äî the board-mode kill self-heal (a window-killing ‚úï collapses a pin-session with no `board-changed` event) calls it to drop the now-dead tile |
| `usePinActions(board?)` | `hooks/use-pin-actions.ts` | `{ pin, unpin, reorder }` stable callbacks; optimistic ‚Äî SSE re-broadcast reconciles. `pin` on success writes last-used (`writeLastPinnedBoard`) and fires the `info` "Pinned to <board>" + "View board" toast (`260718-gxrq`, ¬ß Post-pin success feedback); `unpin`/`reorder` toast on error only (`reorder` rethrows so the caller can roll back its optimistic order) |
| `usePaneWidths(boardName, sidebarWidth)` | `hooks/use-pane-widths.ts` | `{ getWidth, setWidth }`; reads/writes `localStorage["runkit:board-widths:<name>"]`; clamps to `[280, viewport - sidebar]`; default 480px |
| `useBoardAutofit(board)` (`260708-738w`) | `hooks/use-board-autofit.ts` | `{ autofit, toggleAutofit }`; per-board desktop autofit preference in `localStorage["runkit:board-autofit:<board>"]` ("on" sentinel; OFF removes the key); default off; reloads on `board` change (mirrors `usePaneWidths`). Never touches `runkit:board-widths:<board>`. See ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle |
| `useIsMobile()` | `hooks/use-is-mobile.ts` | `boolean`; `matchMedia("(max-width: 640px)")` listener |
| `useActiveBoardName()` | `hooks/use-active-board.ts` | active board name from `/board/<name>` route, else `null` |
| `useWindowPins(server, windowId)` | `hooks/use-window-pins.ts` | list of boards the window is pinned to; drives the pin-icon filled state |
| `useNow()` | `hooks/use-now.ts` | current epoch seconds (`Math.floor(Date.now()/1000)`); self-ticks every 1s via `setInterval` (cleared on unmount), re-rendering ONLY the calling leaf. Display-only clock ‚Äî NOT data polling. Scope to duration leaves so the tick never re-renders ancestors; see ¬ß Render Performance (`260613-ect6`) |
| `useUpdateNotification()` (`260713-4zap`) | `contexts/session-context.tsx` (exported alongside the provider) | `{ qualifies, showChip, tools, key, singleRunKit, latest, current, updateNow, dismissUpdate, daemonVersion, brew, forceUpdateNow, restartNow }` ‚Äî the DERIVED update-notification display shape read by the top-bar `UpdateChip` + the palette `buildUpdateActions`/`buildMaintenanceActions` callers (and the connection-dot title). Reads `SessionContext` via `useContext` DIRECTLY (provider-tolerant ‚Äî never throws outside the provider; each field falls back). `tools` = matched-tool set (`?? EMPTY_TOOLS` frozen module constant, so no per-render array churn); `qualifies = !isDev && tools.length > 0`; `showChip = qualifies && key !== updateDismissedKey` (composite-key dismissal); `singleRunKit` gates the single-run-kit `‚¨Ü v{latest}` wording, `latest`/`current` non-null only then. Self-contained-consumer pattern (mirrors `usePushSubscription`). See ¬ß Update Notification |

## Notifications (Web Push opt-in)

`260615-xd9r-web-push-notifications` adds browser Web Push so `rk notify` (and any process on the box) can deliver an OS notification that reaches the user **even when the RunKit PWA tab is closed**. The end-to-end backend/delivery model lives in `architecture.md` ¬ß Web Push Notifications; this section covers the frontend opt-in surface.

**The opt-in is a Cmd+K palette entry ‚Äî NOT a bell.** Per Constitution ¬ßV (Keyboard-First) and ¬ßIV (Minimal Surface Area, no new route/settings page), the entire opt-in gesture is a single command-palette action. The label reflects subscription state and is **terminal-themed text**, never a bell icon (an explicit user decision ‚Äî a bell was rejected):

| Palette label | When | Action |
|---------------|------|--------|
| `Notifications: Enable push` | Not yet subscribed | Runs the enable flow: `Notification.requestPermission()` ‚Üí on `granted`, `getVapidPublicKey()` (`GET /api/push/vapid-public-key`) ‚Üí `registration.pushManager.subscribe({userVisibleOnly: true, applicationServerKey})` ‚Üí `subscribePush(sub)` (`POST /api/push/subscribe`) |
| `Notifications: Enabled ‚úì` | Already subscribed | Reflects state; the `‚úì` is a Unicode checkmark (terminal-themed glyph, not a bell) |

**Wiring**: `usePushSubscription()` (`app/frontend/src/hooks/use-push-subscription.ts`) returns `{ state, actions }` where `actions` is the `pushActions: PaletteAction[]` block; it is threaded into `app.tsx`'s `paletteActions` useMemo (spread just before `windowSwitchActions` ‚Äî see ¬ß Boards Command Palette for the composition). The flow logic is the self-contained `app/frontend/src/lib/push.ts` module (`registerServiceWorker()`, `enablePushSubscription()`, `getPushState()`) plus the `getVapidPublicKey()`/`subscribePush()` client functions in `api/client.ts` ‚Äî a separate module rather than inlining into the 1600-line, SSE-coupled `app.tsx`. The service worker (`public/sw.js`) is registered on app load from `main.tsx`.

**Fail-silent / secure-context**: every path is throw-free. `registerServiceWorker()` is guarded by `'serviceWorker' in navigator` and no-ops on unsupported / insecure-context environments. The enable flow aborts silently (a toast is acceptable) when permission is denied or push is unsupported / the context is insecure, sending no subscription. Web Push (service worker + `PushManager`) requires a **secure context ‚Äî HTTPS or `localhost`**; the user typically hits run-kit on `localhost:3000` or behind a TLS proxy (both secure), but raw-IP plaintext access simply cannot subscribe (silently).

## Update Notification (`260713-4zap-update-notify-one-click-upgrade`; toolkit-wide `260718-d15e-toolkit-manifest-update-notifications`)

Notifies the web-UI user when a newer release of ANY shll-toolkit tool (run-kit, shll, wt, idea, tu, hop, fab-kit) crosses its per-tool notify threshold, and offers a one-click upgrade that runs a SCOPED `shll update <matched‚Ä¶>` (fallback `rk update` self when shll is absent) ‚Äî brew-upgrading the matched tools and restarting the daemon when run-kit is among them. **In-app ONLY ‚Äî explicitly NO Web Push** (user-decided: Web Push is reserved for waiting agents; update notices must not buzz phones). Two surfaces ‚Äî a top-bar L3 chip + command-palette actions ‚Äî both self-contained consumers of one context hook, mirroring the `NotificationControl`/`usePushSubscription` precedent (no props threaded through `RootTopBar`‚Üí`TopBar`). The backend origin (SSE `event: version`/`event: update-available`, `POST /api/update`, `internal/updatecheck`) is in [architecture.md](/run-kit/architecture.md) ¬ß SSE Hub / ¬ß API Layer; this section is the frontend surface.

### Context state + `useUpdateNotification()` hook

`SessionContext` (`contexts/session-context.tsx`) owns the update state (it already owns the server-global SSE pool + `?metrics=1` stream, and `version`/`update-available` are server-global like `server-order`/`board-order`, so this reuses the exact fan-out ‚Äî no second context). It exposes:

- `daemonVersion: string | null` ‚Äî the running daemon version from `event: version` (no leading `v`), `null` until first seen.
- `updateAvailable: UpdateAvailable | null` ‚Äî the current toolkit-update verdict from `event: update-available`, `null` when none. `UpdateAvailable = { tools: UpdateTool[], key: string, current: string, latest: string }`: `tools` = each matched `{ tool, current, latest }`; `key` = the composite dismissal key (sorted `tool@latest` pairs, comma-joined); `current`/`latest` = the legacy run-kit-row fields, populated only when run-kit is in the match set (transitional not-yet-reloaded-frontend compat).
- `updateDismissedKey: string | null` ‚Äî the composite-key dismissal from localStorage `runkit-update-dismissed` (const `UPDATE_DISMISSED_KEY`), lazily read in a try/catch on mount.
- `updateNow(): Promise<void>` ‚Äî thin wrapper over the `triggerUpdate()` client helper (`POST /api/update`; rejects on non-2xx).
- `dismissUpdate(): void` ‚Äî writes the current `updateAvailable.key` to localStorage `runkit-update-dismissed` + sets `updateDismissedKey`; a no-op on an empty key.
- **`brew: boolean`** ‚Äî whether the daemon is a Homebrew install, from the `event: version` `brew` field. Tracked in React `useState` (`isBrew`, drives palette visibility ‚Üí must re-render, unlike the reload-decision refs below), **default `false` until the first version event is observed** (so the brew-gated `run-kit: Update Now` palette entry stays hidden on the brief pre-connect window; mirrors the `qualifies` absent-data-hidden gating). Set inside `applyVersion`.
- **`forceUpdateNow(): Promise<void>`** ‚Äî thin wrapper over `triggerForceUpdate()` (`POST /api/update` body `{"force":true}`; rejects on non-2xx). Same shape as `updateNow`.
- **`restartNow(): Promise<void>`** ‚Äî thin wrapper over `triggerRestart()` (`POST /api/restart`; rejects on non-2xx).

The `version`/`update-available` listeners are added on **BOTH** stream kinds ‚Äî the per-server pool AND the dedicated `?metrics=1` subscription ‚Äî server-global, applied idempotently (no `data.server` filter), exactly like `server-order`/`board-order`. Both call the pure-ish `applyVersion` / `applyUpdateAvailable` callbacks; malformed events are skipped. **`applyVersion(version, boot, brew)`** parses the payload as `{ version?, boot?, brew? }` **tolerantly** ‚Äî `boot` passed only when `typeof data.boot === "string"` (else `null`), `brew` as `data.brew === true` (defaults `false`) ‚Äî so an older daemon's boot-less/brew-less payload never breaks parsing or flips brew true. **`applyUpdateAvailable(next)`** stores `next` but **dedups by composite `key`** (a re-delivery of the same matched set does not churn consumers) ‚Äî AND handles a **CLEARED payload** (empty `key`) by clearing the stored state so the chip hides. It MUST NOT early-return on an empty key: a siblings-only `shll update` never restarts the daemon, so the post-remediation re-check's cleared `update-available` is the ONLY signal that clears the consumed match; an early return would leave a consumed match advertised forever.

**Tolerant `useUpdateNotification()` hook** (exported from `session-context.tsx`) ‚Äî reads the context via `useContext(SessionContext)` DIRECTLY (not `useSessionContext`, so it **never throws outside the provider**; every field falls back ‚Äî `updateNow`/`forceUpdateNow`/`restartNow` ‚Üí `() => Promise.resolve()`, `dismissUpdate` ‚Üí `() => {}`, `brew` ‚Üí `false`). It returns the DERIVED display shape the chip + palette consume, so the gating logic lives in one place:

- `isDev = daemonVersion === DEV_VERSION` (`"dev"`).
- `tools = updateAvailable?.tools ?? EMPTY_TOOLS` ‚Äî a **module-level frozen `EMPTY_TOOLS` constant** (`Object.freeze([])` cast through `unknown` to the mutable `UpdateTool[]` contract ‚Äî frozen at runtime for a real no-mutation guarantee, typed mutable so the cast doesn't ripple through `updateChipToolSummary`/`buildUpdateActions` consumers) so `?? EMPTY_TOOLS` never mints a new array per render (a fresh `[]` would break referential memoization downstream).
- `key = updateAvailable?.key ?? null`.
- `singleRunKit = tools.length === 1 && tools[0].tool === "run-kit"` (`RUN_KIT_TOOL`) ‚Äî the one shape that keeps the historical single-version chip/palette wording.
- `latest = singleRunKit ? tools[0].latest : null` / `current = singleRunKit ? tools[0].current : null` ‚Äî the run-kit-row versions, surfaced ONLY for the single-run-kit `‚¨Ü v{latest}` chip + `run-kit: Update to v{latest}` palette wording. Null otherwise (a multi/non-run-kit chip uses the count form + per-tool detail).
- **`qualifies = !isDev && tools.length > 0`** ‚Äî the frontend trusts the server's `update-available` verdict for the per-tool threshold decision (the backend already applied it); it only additionally suppresses the `dev` daemon and requires a non-empty matched set. It does NOT re-run any semver compare.
- **`showChip = qualifies && key !== updateDismissedKey`** ‚Äî the chip's composite-key dismissal gate. A later check with a DIFFERENT key (a newly-matching tool or a newer latest) re-shows the chip, because the changed key re-broadcasts `update-available` ‚Üí `updateDismissedKey` no longer equals `key`.
- Returns `{ qualifies, showChip, tools, key, singleRunKit, latest, current, updateNow, dismissUpdate, daemonVersion, brew, forceUpdateNow, restartNow }`. `daemonVersion` is surfaced raw because `buildMaintenanceActions` does its own `version === "dev"` gate.

### Reload guard ‚Äî `shouldReloadOnVersion` (post-restart auto-reload, boot-aware since `260714-3law`)

After a one-click upgrade the daemon restarts, which drops the state socket (since `260716-qf3j-state-socket`; was the SSE connection); the reconnect replays a **different** `version` global event (the same set-once cached slot, now delivered once after `hello` over `/ws/state` ‚Äî see `architecture.md` ¬ß State Socket), and the open tab is now stale (it embeds the old frontend assets baked into the old binary). The guard auto-reloads it exactly once. The reconnect-delivers-the-signal mechanism is unchanged by the transport swap ‚Äî the `StateSocket`'s resubscribe-on-reconnect replays the global slots, so the `version` listener fires exactly as it did over SSE. **Since `260714-3law-force-update-restart-palette` the guard also fires on a same-version restart** (a plain `POST /api/restart`, a config-change/wedge-recovery restart, or a restart initiated from SSH) via the per-process `boot` id ‚Äî so a tab that reconnects to a **new process at the same version** is no longer left silently running stale in-memory state:

- The pure exported predicate is now **4-arg**: `shouldReloadOnVersion(firstVersion: string | null, firstBoot: string | null, nextVersion: string, nextBoot: string | null): boolean` (widened from the pre-`3law` 2-arg `shouldReloadOnVersion(firstSeen, next)`). Logic, in order: (1) `firstVersion === null` ‚Üí `false` (**never reload on first connect** ‚Äî no reload loop, the invariant `4zap` established, unchanged); (2) `nextVersion !== firstVersion` ‚Üí `true` (a version change means new assets ‚Äî the original reload trigger); (3) **same version** ‚Üí reload on a **boot change** UNLESS the version is `"dev"`: `nextVersion === DEV_VERSION` returns `false` (the **air-recompile storm guard** ‚Äî under `just dev`, air recompiles the backend on every save, minting a fresh boot id each time; reloading every dev tab on every recompile would be a reload storm; a dev version never changes so version-based reload is moot in practice, but the guard keeps the predicate honest), else `nextBoot !== null && nextBoot !== firstBoot`. A **null `nextBoot`** (older daemon, mixed-version window) never triggers the boot branch.
- `applyVersion(version, boot, brew)` (the `version`-listener callback): sets `daemonVersion` + `isBrew`; if `shouldReloadOnVersion(firstVersionRef.current, firstBootRef.current, version, boot)` ‚Üí `location.reload()` (and returns); else, **only on the first-ever version** (`firstVersionRef.current === null`), stamps BOTH `firstVersionRef.current = version` and `firstBootRef.current = boot`. Both `firstVersionRef` and `firstBootRef` (new in `3law`) are `useRef` (not state ‚Äî the reload decision must not re-render) so `applyVersion` stays referentially stable.
- Coverage this buys: update (version change), plain restart (boot change, same version), every open tab (the version slot is replayed per SSE connect), and restarts initiated from SSH or crash-recovery (the signal is server-originated, not client-action-originated).

### Top-bar L3 UpdateChip (`UpdateChip` in `top-bar.tsx`)

A self-contained chip in the L3 right cluster, **leading `NotificationControl`** (the L3 order is Update ‚Üí Notification ‚Üí Theme ‚Üí Refresh ‚Üí Help ‚Üí connection dot). Reads `useUpdateNotification()`. It is a registry candidate, not a `hidden sm:flex`-wrapped fixture (`260715-h1ck-top-bar-overflow-chevron-menu`): its bar/menu presence is 100% registry-driven (registry `hidden: !showChip` keeps it out of the candidate set when it wouldn't render, so it never reserves width or an empty slot). Below `sm` it does not vanish; under width pressure it overflows into the chevron menu, where its function merges into the fixed version row (¬ß Right cluster overflow / ¬ß Steady-state version surfaces ‚Üí version-row-as-update-surface). The palette update surface remains for keyboard-first parity, and is no longer the only phone surface (the menu reaches it too).

- **Hide gate**: `if (!showChip || tools.length === 0) return null` ‚Äî the hide conditions (no qualifying update / dismissed-for-key / daemon is `dev`) are folded into `showChip` inside the hook.
- **Single/multi presentation** (R15): the visible label is `‚¨Ü v{latest}` when the single matched tool is run-kit (`singleRunKit`), else a count form `‚¨Ü updates (N)` for any other single tool OR multiple tools. The chip runs a SCOPED update of exactly the matched tools, so the `title`/`aria-label` must say WHICH tools move: `restLabel = singleRunKit && current ? `Update run-kit: v{current} ‚Üí v{latest}` : `Update: ${updateChipToolSummary(tools)}``, where `updateChipToolSummary` composes the per-tool `tool v{a} ‚Üí v{b}` transitions (a tool with no known current degrades to `tool ‚Üí v{latest}`). Accent styling (`border-accent-green text-accent-green` + `rk-glint` CRT-glint hover ‚Äî the button hover vocabulary, ¬ß Hover-Animation Vocabulary).
- **Click ‚Üí one-click trigger** via the shared **`useUpdateClick()`** hook (`hooks/use-update-click.ts`), consumed by BOTH the chip and the overflow-menu version-row update surface so the updating-state + failure catch/toast is ONE implementation, never a mirrored copy. `triggerUpdate` early-returns if already `updating`, records the composite `key` at click time (`clickKeyRef`), sets `updating`, then `void updateNow().catch(...)`. On a request FAILURE (409 not-brew / no-match / network) it clears `updating` + shows an error toast. The busy state renders a `<LogoSpinner size={12}>` + `<span>{"updating‚Ä¶"}</span>` ‚Äî the busy label is a JS string expression (a real `‚Ä¶` U+2026), NOT raw JSX text (JSX text does not process JS escape sequences, so a raw `‚Ä¶` would render six literal chars; `update-chip.test.tsx` asserts the exact visible text `updating‚Ä¶`).
- **Two `updating`-clearing paths** (R13): (1) run-kit IN the spawned scope ‚Üí the daemon restarts, the state socket drops, and the reconnect's differing version reloads the tab (discarding this state); (2) SIBLINGS-ONLY scope ‚Üí NO daemon restart, so no reload comes ‚Äî the post-remediation re-check (R17, architecture ¬ß internal/updatecheck) broadcasts a cleared/changed `update-available` whose composite `key` differs from the click-time key, and a `useEffect` keyed on `key` clears `updating` when `key !== clickKeyRef.current` (including the cleared empty key). A FAILED brew upgrade leaves the key unchanged, so `updating` persists until a page reload / the palette force path ‚Äî the accepted residual (same failure envelope as the old rk-only flow, which relied on a reload that never came).
- **Dismiss `‚úï`**: a small sibling button (rendered only when `!updating`, `aria-label="Dismiss update notice"`) ‚Üí `dismissUpdate()` (composite-key localStorage). Dismissal silences only the chip; the palette action remains (keyboard-first recoverability, ¬ßV).

### Palette parity ‚Äî `run-kit:` actions via `buildUpdateActions` (`lib/palette-update.ts`)

Keyboard-first parity (¬ßV): the pure helper `buildUpdateActions(qualifies, tools, onUpdate, onDismiss): UpdatePaletteAction[]` (in `lib/palette-update.ts`, unit-testable, mirroring `lib/palette-move.ts`) returns, when `qualifies && tools.length > 0`:

- `{ id: "run-kit-update", label: updateActionLabel(tools), onSelect: onUpdate }` ‚Äî the label follows the single/multi split: a single run-kit match reads `run-kit: Update to v{latest}` (historical form); a single non-run-kit tool reads `run-kit: Update {tool} to v{latest}`; multiple tools read `run-kit: Update N tools`. The action always runs a SCOPED update of exactly the matched tools.
- `{ id: "run-kit-dismiss-update", label: "run-kit: Dismiss Update Notice", onSelect: onDismiss }` ‚Äî `onDismiss` writes the composite key.

and an empty array otherwise. **Gated on `qualifies` ALONE ‚Äî the palette deliberately IGNORES chip dismissal** (`qualifies`, NOT the chip's `showChip`): dismissal silences the ambient chip, but the palette is deliberate discovery. The per-tool `updateChipToolSummary` helper (consumed by the chip + overflow-menu aria) is the single exported source in this module, so the top bar and the menu can never drift (R15 / A-024).

**Dual-mount duplication** (the board-palette convention, ¬ß Command Palette View actions ‚Üí Dual-mount duplication): the app mounts TWO CommandPalettes and the board route does NOT render AppShell, so a globally-meaningful action must be registered in both.

- **AppShell palette** (`app.tsx`): an `updateActions` block (a `useMemo` over `buildUpdateActions`, alongside `viewActions`) folded into `paletteActions` after `configActions` and before `serverActions`. The update action wraps `updateNow` with a toast-on-failure handler (`"error"` severity).
- **Board palette** (`board-page.tsx` `boardRouteActions`): `buildUpdateActions` is duplicated in as `updateEntries`, appended near-last (since `260714-3law` the tail is `[...switchEntries, ...conditional, ...fontEntries, refreshEntry, helpEntry, ...updateEntries, ...maintenanceEntries]` ‚Äî the maintenance entries follow the update entries, see below) ‚Äî because below `sm` the top-bar UpdateChip is hidden, so on a phone `/board/$name` the palette is the ONLY update surface. (The board's toast call passes no severity arg, unlike AppShell's `"error"`.)

The Host page (`/`) mounts no palette, so it carries no update palette action (pre-existing scope-out ‚Äî its chip still renders in the mode-invariant right cluster).

### Maintenance palette entries ‚Äî `buildMaintenanceActions` (`lib/palette-update.ts`, `260714-3law-force-update-restart-palette`)

Two **palette-only** maintenance actions, independent of the qualifying-update gate that governs `buildUpdateActions` ‚Äî they exist to make **patch-release update** and **daemon restart** reachable from the web (remote/mobile over Tailscale, no SSH), per Constitution V (keyboard-first) and IV (no new chrome). There is **no chip, no confirmation dialog, and no dedicated toast** ‚Äî both fire immediately on select, and the SSE drop followed by the boot/version-driven tab reload IS the success feedback (only a rejection surfaces a toast).

The pure builder `buildMaintenanceActions(brew: boolean, version: string | null, onForceUpdate, onRestart): UpdatePaletteAction[]` (co-located with `buildUpdateActions` in `lib/palette-update.ts`, same test surface) computes `isDev = version === "dev"` and returns:

- `{ id: "run-kit-force-update", label: "run-kit: Update Now", onSelect: onForceUpdate }` ‚Äî included ONLY when **`brew && !isDev`**. Force update (skips the qualify gate server-side), so it reaches patch releases and works before any check has run. Brew-gated because a non-brew install cannot self-upgrade (the backend brew 409 would reject it anyway).
- `{ id: "run-kit-restart", label: "run-kit: Restart Daemon", onSelect: onRestart }` ‚Äî included whenever **`!isDev`** (**NO brew requirement** ‚Äî restart works for any install method).

Neither appears on a `dev` daemon (both gated on `!isDev`). The existing qualifying-gated `run-kit: Update to v{latest}` entry (`buildUpdateActions`) is **unchanged** ‚Äî a slight label overlap when an update qualifies is an accepted tradeoff (two static labels beat dynamic ones).

**Dual-mounted** per the same board-palette duplication convention as `buildUpdateActions` (below `sm` the top-bar chip cluster is hidden, so board routes on phones need palette parity ‚Äî and there is no chip surface for these two at all):

- **AppShell** (`app.tsx`): a `maintenanceActions` `useMemo` over `buildMaintenanceActions(brew, daemonVersion, ‚Ä¶)` (reading `brew`/`daemonVersion`/`forceUpdateNow`/`restartNow` from `useUpdateNotification()`), folded into `paletteActions` right after `updateActions`. Each action wraps `forceUpdateNow`/`restartNow` in a `.catch` toast-on-failure with **`"error"` severity** (messages `"Update failed"` / `"Restart failed"`).
- **Board** (`board-page.tsx` `boardRouteActions`): `maintenanceEntries` via the same builder + gating, appended **last** after `updateEntries`, with the same `.catch` toast handling but **no severity arg** (mirroring the board's existing `updateEntries` convention).

### Steady-state version surfaces (`260715-ifco-expose-running-version-ui`)

The `UpdateChip` above renders **only when a qualifying update is pending** and names only the TARGET version, so the running version is otherwise **invisible in the web UI** ‚Äî a user filing a bug report or verifying a restart had to SSH in for `rk --version`. `260715-ifco` adds **four passive, chrome-level surfaces** that expose the *current* `daemonVersion` in steady state (frontend-only ‚Äî the version already reaches every tab via `event: version`; no backend, no new routes/pages/buttons per Constitution IV, palette-first per V) ‚Äî and `260715-h1ck` adds a **fifth**, the overflow menu's fixed version row (surface 5 below). All **degrade gracefully on a null `daemonVersion`** (hide/omit, never a `vundefined` placeholder) and show the **`dev` sentinel as-is** (`run-kit dev`, not `vdev`) ‚Äî pure display, unlike the dev-gated update/restart actions.

**Shared `displayVersion` helper + `lib/palette-version.ts`.** A new pure, dependency-free module `app/frontend/src/lib/palette-version.ts` (mirroring the `lib/palette-update.ts` pattern, colocated `palette-version.test.ts`) exports:

- **`displayVersion(version: string): string`** ‚Äî the single frontend source of the v-prefix convention, mirroring the backend `displayVersion()` (`app/backend/cmd/rk/root.go:16-21`): prefixes `v` to a numeric version, leaves `dev` and any already-`v`-prefixed string bare (idempotent ‚Äî never `vdev` / `vv0.6.2`). Reused by all three display surfaces below (avoids the magic-string conditional per-site). Chosen to live in the palette module rather than a standalone `lib/version.ts` ‚Äî the palette builder already needs it and it is the new dependency-free home.
- **`buildVersionAction(version: string | null, onSelect: () => void): VersionPaletteAction[]`** ‚Äî returns `[]` when `version` is null (omit, no placeholder), else a single `{ id: "run-kit-version", label: `run-kit: Version ‚Äî ${displayVersion(version)}`, onSelect }`. The LABEL carries the version, so typing "version" in the palette answers "what am I on?" **without selecting anything**. `VersionPaletteAction` is a local type mirroring `palette-update.ts`'s shape.

**1. Command-palette version entry** (the primary discovery surface, ¬ßV). `buildVersionAction` is **dual-mounted** ‚Äî the same board-palette duplication convention as the update actions (¬ß Dual-mount duplication), and for the same reason: below `sm` the top-bar right cluster is hidden, so on a phone `/board/$name` the palette is the ONLY version surface.
  - **AppShell** (`app.tsx`): a `versionActions` `useMemo` over `buildVersionAction(daemonVersion, ‚Ä¶)`, folded into `paletteActions` **after `maintenanceActions`, before `serverActions`**.
  - **Board** (`board-page.tsx` `boardRouteActions`): `versionEntries` via the same builder, appended **last** after `maintenanceEntries` (`[...switchEntries, ...conditional, ...fontEntries, refreshEntry, helpEntry, ...updateEntries, ...maintenanceEntries, ...versionEntries]`).
  - **Gated on non-null `daemonVersion` INCLUDING `dev`** ‚Äî `buildVersionAction`'s only gate is the null check (pure display; the entry is present for a `dev` daemon).
  - **On select**: copies the **DISPLAYED form** (`v0.6.2` / `dev` ‚Äî what-you-see-is-what-you-copy, matches the label; NOT the raw `daemonVersion`) via `lib/clipboard.ts` `copyToClipboard`, then toasts. AppShell: `addToast(ok ? "Version copied" : "Copy failed", ok ? "info" : "error")`. Board: `addToast("Version copied", "info")` on success / `addToast("Copy failed")` (no severity arg) on failure ‚Äî matching the board's own `updateEntries`/`maintenanceEntries` toast convention.

**2. Connection-dot version title** ‚Äî the top-bar dot's hover `title` folds in `Connected ‚Äî run-kit {displayVersion(daemonVersion)}`; full mechanics in ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) ‚Üí Connection dot.

**3. Host-page footer stamp** (`host-overview-page.tsx`) ‚Äî a small passive BIOS/boot-style footer line `run-kit {displayVersion(daemonVersion)}` at the **bottom of the scroll container, after the SERVICES `</section>`** (out of the zone hierarchy ‚Äî a POST-footer, on-brand with the CRT/terminal aesthetic). `text-xs text-text-secondary font-mono`, no border, no interaction, **no hover treatment** (passive means passive ‚Äî the hover-animation vocabulary categories don't apply to inert text). Reads `daemonVersion` from `useSessionContext()` and renders **nothing when null** (`{daemonVersion && (‚Ä¶)}`, absence not a hidden placeholder). The Host page `/` is the only route with no top-bar version surface on phones, and its BIOS-footer aesthetic fits the stamp best.

**4. UpdateChip transition title** ‚Äî the pending-update chip's `title`/`aria-label` now show `v{current} ‚Üí v{latest}`; mechanics in ¬ß Top-bar L3 UpdateChip and the `current` field in ¬ß Context state + `useUpdateNotification()` hook.

**5. Overflow menu's fixed version row** (`260715-h1ck-top-bar-overflow-chevron-menu`, `top-bar-overflow-menu.tsx`) ‚Äî the top-bar overflow chevron's menu **always** contains a fixed version row as its last item (so the chevron renders even when nothing overflows; full mechanics in ¬ß Right cluster ‚Üí overflow chevron menu). It reuses the same `displayVersion(daemonVersion)` + `copyToClipboard` machinery as the palette version action: renders `Run Kit v{version}`, click copies the DISPLAYED form and toasts (`"Version copied"` / `"Copy failed"`); renders plain `Run Kit` ‚Äî no `v`, no `vundefined` ‚Äî when `daemonVersion` is null. This is the sixth home of `displayVersion` and a chrome (not palette) version surface reachable on touch at any width. **Version-row-as-update-surface** (the surface-4 UpdateChip's overflow twin): when a qualifying update is pending AND the UpdateChip is currently overflowed into this same menu, the version row FLIPS from copy-mode to update-mode ‚Äî it shows `Run Kit v{current} ‚Üí v{latest} ‚¨Ü` and click triggers the update (`updateNow()`) instead of copying, and no separate UpdateChip menu row is added (its function merges here). The chevron carries an accent attention badge in this state so the overflowed update signal is not lost. Both the chip and this row consume the shared `useUpdateClick()` hook (`hooks/use-update-click.ts`), so the updating-state + failure catch/toast is ONE implementation, never a mirrored copy.

**`copyToClipboard` success signal.** `lib/clipboard.ts` `copyToClipboard` was **widened from `Promise<void>` to `Promise<boolean>`** ‚Äî `true` on a successful copy (Clipboard API OR the `execCommand` non-secure-context fallback), `false` when both fail (previously the total-failure branch silently swallowed the error). This is a **backwards-compatible** change: the pre-existing callers (`terminal-client.tsx`, `status-panel.tsx`) `void`-ignore the return and are unaffected; the new palette-version `onSelect` consumes the boolean to toast confirmation vs. error (honoring "fail soft with an error toast" in a non-secure context). The `copyToClipboard` return-value cases (Clipboard-API success, `execCommand`-fallback success, total failure) are unit-tested in `terminal-client.test.ts` (the pre-existing home of the `copyToClipboard` describe block ‚Äî no separate `clipboard.test.ts` was added).

## Shell Grid Layout

The `<Shell>` wrapper (`app/frontend/src/components/shell/shell.tsx`) is the shared layout for `AppShell` and `BoardPage` (the Host page `/` uses a plain `flex-col h-full` instead ‚Äî no Shell). **Since `260707-4vq2-lift-topbar-root-layout` the Shell grid NO LONGER carries a `topbar` row** ‚Äî the TopBar is lifted out of every per-page grid and mounts once in the persistent root layout, full-width above the Shell (see ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) ‚Üí persistent root mount). Because the pre-`4vq2` grid already spanned the topbar full-width above the sidebar, dropping the row and painting the bar above Shell from the root layout is a **geometric no-op** ‚Äî the visual stack (full-width bar over sidebar+content) is preserved.

The **desktop** (`‚â• 640px`) grid is now just sidebar+content over bottombar:

```
gridTemplateAreas: "sidebar content" / "sidebar bottombar"   (rows: 1fr auto)
```

`gridTemplateColumns` stays `${sidebarWidth}px 1fr` when `sidebarOpen` else `0 1fr` (a `150ms ease-out` collapse transition, zero-width column when closed ‚Äî no rail). The **mobile** (`< 640px`) branch is single-column `gridTemplateAreas: "content" "bottombar"` (rows `1fr auto`), with the sidebar rendered as an `absolute` overlay whose grid child spans `gridRow: "1 / 3"` (the content+bottombar rows, re-indexed from the pre-`4vq2` `"2 / 4"` now that the topbar row is gone ‚Äî see ¬ß Sidebar Mobile). Children place themselves via `style={{ gridArea: ‚Ä¶ }}`.

**Shell height is `100%`** (was `var(--app-height, 100vh)` pre-`4vq2`) ‚Äî Shell fills the root layout's `flex-1` content region rather than sizing itself to the viewport. Shell no longer calls `useVisualViewport()` or consumes `--app-height` directly (both moved to `RootWrapper` ‚Äî see ¬ß iOS Keyboard Support). `useSidebarKeyboardToggle` (Cmd+\ / Ctrl+\) stays registered in Shell with unchanged behavior ‚Äî the chord is live only on routes that mount a `<Shell>` (AppShell + BoardPage), as before.

**History**: since `260702-6m46-full-width-topbar-navbar` the topbar had spanned BOTH columns (`"topbar topbar" / "sidebar content" / "sidebar bottombar"`, rows `auto 1fr auto`, mobile `"topbar" "content" "bottombar"`); before `260702-6m46` it shared row 1 with the sidebar (`"sidebar topbar"`). `260707-4vq2` removed the row entirely and rewrote the `shell.tsx` ASCII topology comment to match.

## Chrome (Top Bar)

The full-width top bar is the app's primary chrome and doubles as the navbar. **Since `260707-4vq2-lift-topbar-root-layout` it mounts ONCE at the persistent root layout, above the router `<Outlet>` ‚Äî not once per page** (see ¬ß Persistent root mount below). `TopBar` (`app/frontend/src/components/top-bar.tsx`) accepts a `mode: "terminal" | "board" | "server" | "host"` prop (default `"terminal"`) selecting the left-nav content; the `260702-6m46-full-width-topbar-navbar` change added the host mode (then named `"cockpit"`, renamed to `"host"` in `260715-zs1y`) and turned the left nav into a breadcrumb bar. Everything below (per-mode breadcrumbs, center heading, right-cluster pyramid, connection dot) describes `TopBar`'s internal rendering, which `4vq2` did NOT touch ‚Äî it relocated the mount only. *(The page-mode strings were renamed in `260715-zs1y`: `"cockpit"` ‚Üí `"host"` (`/`) and `"root"` ‚Üí `"server"` (`/$server`); the canonical page names became Host / tmux Server. This section is written throughout in the new vocabulary.)*

### Persistent root mount (`RootTopBar` / `AppLayout`, `260707-4vq2-lift-topbar-root-layout`)

Pre-`4vq2`, `TopBar` was mounted **three times** ‚Äî once inside each page component (`AppShell` for `/$server` + `/$server/$window`, `HostOverviewPage` for `/`, `BoardPage` for `/board/$name`) ‚Äî so cross-page navigation unmounted one instance and mounted a fresh one, a visible navbar "reload"/flicker (the app is already an SPA; this was a component-identity problem, not an MPA‚ÜíSPA gap). `4vq2` lifts the bar to a single persistent mount that re-renders in place across route changes.

**Where it mounts.** A **pathless layout route** (`id: "app-layout"`, `router.tsx`) uniformly parents every page route (index, server, terminal, board), so every navigation keeps the match chain `[root, app-layout, <leaf>]`. Its component `AppLayout` (`app.tsx`) sits at a **stable match depth with a stable route id and is never remounted** across navigation; it renders a flex column ‚Äî `<div className="app-root flex flex-col" style={{ height: "var(--app-height, 100vh)" }}>` ‚Äî with `RootTopBar` in a `shrink-0` wrapper above a `flex-1 min-h-0` content region. The bar keeps a stable React identity and re-renders (props change, no unmount) as the URL flips. (Hosting the bar directly in `RootWrapper` ‚Äî the root route's component ‚Äî was tried and rejected: the index route `/` is a direct child of the root at the same pathname, making the root‚Üíindex chain structurally shorter than root‚ÜíserverLayout‚Üí‚Ä¶, so React remounted the root subtree on the index-route transition. The pathless layout normalizes tree depth and removes that asymmetry.) The `AppLayout` wrapper is a plain `div`, NOT `<header>` ‚Äî `TopBar` already renders its own `<header>` banner landmark, so a second would nest two `role="banner"` landmarks.

**Suspense blast radius.** The `<Suspense fallback={null}>` boundary now wraps ONLY the `<Outlet>` content region (inside `AppLayout`), not the header. So when the lazy board chunk loads, only the page body blanks ‚Äî the bar stays painted (fixing the second flicker cause without touching the lazy-loading strategy; `fallback={null}` itself is unchanged).

**Prop delivery ‚Äî two channels.** `TopBar`'s inputs split by how synchronously they must resolve:

- **Route-derived (synchronous, at root)**: `RootTopBar` (`app.tsx`) derives `mode` + `boardName` from `useMatches()` ‚Äî a deepest-first walk over route params (`window` ‚áí `terminal`, `name` ‚áí `board` + `boardName`, `server` ‚áí `server`, none ‚áí `host`; param names are unique across the tree, the same walk `SessionContext` uses for `currentServer`). This flips the instant the URL changes, so the heading never waits on the incoming page's mount ‚Äî critical for the lazy board (`Board: <name>` renders from the URL param while the chunk still loads). `mode`/`boardName` are deliberately NOT in the slot.
- **Page-registered (a slot context, `contexts/top-bar-slot-context.tsx`)**: pages publish their data/handler props ‚Äî `sessions`, `currentSession`, `currentWindow`, `sessionName`, `windowName`, `isConnected`, `sidebarOpen`, `server`, `onNavigate`, `onToggleSidebar`, `onCreateSession`, `onCreateWindow`, plus board extras (`paneCount`, `serverCount`, `waitingPaneCount`, `boards`, `focusedPane` ‚Äî the focused-tile split target ‚Äî `onRequestKill` ‚Äî the board ‚úï's kill-dialog opener, `260718-co9z`, replacing the removed direct-kill `onPaneClosed` seam (itself `260715-6jwn`'s replacement of the earlier `onCloseFocused`/`closeDisabled` unpin pair) ‚Äî and ‚Äî `260708-738w` ‚Äî `autofit`/`onToggleAutofit` for the board autofit toggle, ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle) ‚Äî via `useRegisterTopBarSlot(...)` (an effect: publish on mount/update, **clear to `null` on unmount**, last-writer-wins). This follows the `FocusedTerminalProvider` precedent (referentially-stable dispatcher held in a `useRef`, `useMemo`'d context value) and keeps the heavy handlers where they live ‚Äî `AppShell`'s `navigateToWindow` (View-Transitions gate) and `handleCreateSessionInstant` (optimistic ghosts) are published by reference; **no logic migrates to root**.

**Tolerant-empty defaults.** When no page has registered yet (first frame after navigation, or a lazy chunk still loading), the slot value is `null` and `RootTopBar` renders the route-derived mode with the tolerant-empty prop shape every `TopBar` mode already supports (`sessions=[]`, `currentSession=null`, `currentWindow=null`, `sessionName/windowName/server=""`, `sidebarOpen=false`, no-op callbacks). No crash, no stale props from the prior page (the clear-on-unmount guarantees this).

**Not-found is a dedicated boolean channel.** `TopBarSlotContext` carries a `notFound` flag SEPARATE from the page-data `slot`. `NotFoundPage` (`router.tsx`) ‚Äî the `app-layout` route's `notFoundComponent`, rendered inside the `<Outlet>` below the persistent bar ‚Äî calls `useSignalTopBarNotFound()` (sets `true` on mount / `false` on unmount); `RootTopBar` reads `useTopBarNotFound()` and forces `mode="host"` (nulling `boardName`) BEFORE the route-param walk. This is required because TanStack Router's fuzzy not-found handling RETAINS the partially-matched params in `useMatches()` (e.g. `/board/x/y` keeps `name=x`), so the param walk alone would derive `board` mode ("Board: x") over the not-found body. A separate boolean (vs. folding into the page-data slot, or reading the router's internal `globalNotFound`) keeps `NotFoundPage` ‚Äî which owns no TopBar data ‚Äî from publishing the full slot shape, and avoids coupling to a router-internal field + hardcoded route-id string. Because `RootTopBar` sits ABOVE the `<Outlet>`, the in-Outlet signal is inherently one render behind: a ~1-frame "Board: x" flash before the effect lands is unavoidable without reading router internals ‚Äî not user-perceptible, and the settled state (A-015) is unaffected. (The `/a/b/c` shape is a DIFFERENT arm: it renders `AppShell`'s `ServerNotFound` early-return, not `NotFoundPage`, so `notFound` stays false there and the `server`/`terminal` mode derivation is kept.)

**Per-page removal.** Each page dropped its `<TopBar>` mount and registers instead: `AppShell` deleted its `<header style={{ gridArea: "topbar" }}><TopBar/></header>` block and its `topBarMode` local (the `terminal` vs `server` distinction is now derived at root); `HostOverviewPage` deleted its `<TopBar mode="host"/>` mount + import and registers just `isConnected: hostMetricsConnected` (its wrapper `flex flex-col h-screen` ‚Üí `h-full`); `BoardPage` deleted its board `<header>‚Ä¶<TopBar mode="board"/>` block (kept the `HELP_URL` import for its palette action) and registers the board extras (`boardName`, counts, `boards`, `focusedPane`, and since `260718-co9z` `onRequestKill: requestKillFocused` ‚Äî the kill-dialog opener replacing the removed direct-kill `onPaneClosed: handlePaneClosed` seam ‚Äî `isConnected: boardConnected`). Edge pages (`NotFoundPage`, `ServerNotFound`, `ServerWaiting`) changed their centering wrapper `h-screen` ‚Üí `h-full` so they fit the content region below the persistent bar without overflow.

**Achievable-invariant note (e2e).** No component in the persistent chain (`RootWrapper`/`AppLayout`/`RootTopBar`/`TopBar`) remounts across navigation, so the flicker is gone and the bar stays continuously present with a per-route heading ‚Äî this is what `tests/e2e/top-bar-persistence.spec.ts` asserts (mount-effect stability + per-route heading), NOT strict DOM-node identity. TanStack Router 1.168's per-match Suspense re-commit recreates the header host node on the `‚Üí /` (index-route) transition; that is a router-internal reconciliation artifact that does NOT remount the component and does NOT blank the bar (the heading renders synchronously from route state), so it is not a user-visible flicker. The spec's brand-crumb hop is a RELOAD BOUNDARY ‚Äî the brand is a raw `<a href="/">` TanStack Router does not intercept, a full document navigation ‚Äî so only the client-side hops carry the no-remount claim.

**Non-goals.** Sidebar/BottomBar/Shell stay per-page (they still remount on `/$server` ‚Üî `/board/$name`); `TopBar`'s internal rendering across all four modes is unchanged; frontend-only (no backend/API/tmux change).

`app.tsx` and `board-page.tsx` no longer render `<TopBar>` directly; `host-overview-page.tsx` (Host page `/`) no longer pins it above its own scroll container. All three now register into the slot context (see ¬ß Persistent root mount above). The right-section control cluster is a **strict 3-level cumulative pyramid** (`260704-9o7k-top-bar-button-pyramid`): a stable always-block pinned right renders in every mode, with terminal+board extras and terminal-only extras growing leftward ‚Äî so no shared button ever changes screen position between pages. Only which levels appear gates on mode; see ¬ß Right cluster below.

**Layout** (`border-b-[3px] border-border` ‚Äî a 3px structural seam, see ¬ß Border-Width System): a single line, a **3-column CSS grid `grid grid-cols-[1fr_auto_1fr] items-center gap-2 py-2`** (since `260703-5ilm-window-heading-hover-vocabulary` replaced the former `flex justify-between`). The grid is the load-bearing change: `1fr auto 1fr` makes the CENTER cell truly centered regardless of asymmetric left/right widths, which `flex justify-between` could not do. LEFT cell = `<nav aria-label="Breadcrumb">` (ends at the parent ‚Äî see per-mode below); CENTER cell = the **universal `PageType: name` page heading, FILLED IN EVERY MODE** since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` (terminal `WindowHeading` + ‚ñæ window switcher / board display heading + ‚ñæ board switcher / server display heading / solo `Host` ‚Äî the cell is no longer empty on server/board/host; ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell); RIGHT cell = the control cluster (`justify-self-end`). No Line 2. The header itself carries `px-3` (the center cell is `flex items-center justify-center min-w-0`, no flex `gap` ‚Äî the boot sweep owns the prefix‚Üíname spacing via its own space cell).

**Brand root crumb** (all modes, left-most): the logo icon (`/icon.svg`, always visible) + `hidden sm:inline` "Run Kit" wordmark wrapped in a single `<a href="/">` (`aria-label="Run Kit home"`). This IS the home affordance ‚Äî there is no separate "Host" crumb, and the old right-side "Run Kit" anchor is GONE (moved here by `260702-6m46`). The brand carries the `LINK_CRUMB_CLASS` bordered-chip treatment (see ¬ß Crumb Affordance Vocabulary). Below `sm` it collapses to the bare icon so long crumbs still fit the single-line 375px topbar.

**Hamburger** ‚Äî the sidebar toggle (`aria-label="Toggle navigation"`, a Notion-style rounded-rect pictogram whose left column fills when `sidebarOpen`). Renders BETWEEN the brand and the first crumb, on every mode that has a sidebar. `hasSidebar` is DERIVED as `mode !== "host"` (no separate prop) ‚Äî the host mode is the only sidebar-less mode, so it gets no hamburger.

**Separator** ‚Äî `‚Ä∫` (U+203A, `aria-hidden`, `BreadcrumbSeparator`), the established palette-label convention (`<session> ‚Ä∫ <name>`). It replaced the old `/` plain-text separator (removed by `260702-6m46`) between every crumb level. No `/` separator remains.

**Host** (`/`, `mode="host"`): brand crumb ONLY ‚Äî no hamburger, no crumbs, no terminal-font control, no split/close buttons, and **no fixed-width button** (terminal-only since `260704-9o7k`; the 900px effect never applied to the Host page ‚Äî `host-overview-page.tsx` never reads `fixedWidth`). Renders only the L3 always-block (Notification / Theme / Refresh / Help) **plus the connection dot**, which since `260704-9o7k` reflects **host-metrics stream health** (formerly hidden here on the premise "no per-server SSE stream"; the Host page's live data actually arrives via the dedicated `?metrics=1` stream or the per-server metrics fan-out ‚Äî `host-overview-page.tsx` passes `hostMetricsConnected` from `useSessionContext()`, replacing the old `isConnected={false}`; see ¬ß Right cluster ‚Üí connection dot and architecture.md ¬ß Server-independent host-metrics subscription). Session/server-dependent props are passed empty (`sessions=[]`, `currentSession=null`, `currentWindow=null`, `sessionName=""`, `server=""`, no-op callbacks) ‚Äî the same tolerant-empty shape board mode uses. The Host page's page identity is the **solo `Host` heading in the top-bar center cell** since `260704-pr0p` (a `PageHeadingDisplay` with `prefix=""` + `name="Host"` + `solo` ‚Äî primary-medium, visible at all breakpoints; ¬ß center cell), plus the in-page `Host Overview` SectionHeading added by `260715-zs1y` (¬ß Page Overview Headings). The former in-page `[ cockpit ]` `PageHeading` row (retired under the old vocabulary) is GONE. A "Run Kit Host" doubled word was rejected ‚Äî it would duplicate the adjacent brand crumb.

**tmux Server** (`/$server`, no `$window`, `mode="server"`): the left breadcrumb ends at **brand + hamburger** ‚Äî nothing more. Since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` the server name is the **`tmux Server: <server>` heading in the CENTER cell** (a display-only `PageHeadingDisplay`, no rename), NOT a left-nav leaf. The former `260702-6m46` server-mode leaf ‚Äî a non-link `<span aria-current="page">` server name (which had itself replaced the deleted literal "Dashboard" label) ‚Äî was REMOVED from the left nav (move-don't-copy: the current-page leaf is the centered heading; a name never appears twice in the bar). "Dashboard" still appears nowhere.

**Terminal** (`/$server/$window`, `mode="terminal"`): the breadcrumb is brand + hamburger + `‚Ä∫` + server link + `‚Ä∫` + **session dropdown ‚Äî and ENDS THERE** (since `260703-5ilm` the window identity moved OUT of the breadcrumb chain into the centered `WindowHeading`; the former trailing `‚Ä∫` + window dropdown are gone from the left nav). The server crumb here is a plain `<a href="/$server">` (a link back to the tmux Server page, `LINK_CRUMB_CLASS` chip, `truncate max-w-[16ch]`) ‚Äî NOT a dropdown (server switching stays in the command palette, `Server: Switch to ‚Ä¶`). The session crumb keeps its existing `BreadcrumbDropdown` behavior unchanged (session switch jumps to the session's first window; `+ New Session` action; session `max-w-[16ch] truncate` (matches the server crumb); the session name is snapshot-derived from the active `@N`, not a URL segment, since `260529-jad6`). **The window switcher relocated to the center cell** ‚Äî a label-less bare-`‚ñæ` `BreadcrumbDropdown` (still `title="Window"`, still `windowItems` + `+ New Window` action) sitting beside the `WindowHeading` (name-click = edit, `‚ñæ`-click = switch), so the window name is never duplicated in one bar. Since `260704-pr0p` the centered `WindowHeading` gains a static prefix sibling span (¬ß Window Heading) ‚Äî the two-tone `PageType: name` identity, `Window:` in every lens since `260714-uco1` ‚Äî but the breadcrumb shape is otherwise unchanged (this is the only mode whose left nav did NOT lose a leaf to the generalized move-don't-copy rule, because it already ended at the session crumb). See ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell / ¬ß Breadcrumb Dropdowns ‚Üí Window switcher. No type-prefix words ("SERVER"/"tmux Server"/"session") ‚Äî crumbs are instance names only; position conveys the level. The level IS named on hover via native `title` tooltips in the canonical vocabulary: brand `title="Host"`, server crumb `title="tmux Server"` (both link and leaf variants), session dropdown trigger `title="Session"` and the relocated window switcher `title="Window"` (via BreadcrumbDropdown's optional `title` prop).

**Center cell ‚Äî the universal `PageType: name` page heading** (`260703-5ilm` introduced it terminal-only; `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` FILLED IT ON EVERY MODE). The outer center `<div className="flex items-center justify-center min-w-0">` (no flex `gap` ‚Äî the boot sweep's own `sp` space cell separates prefix from name; a `gap-1` on top double-spaced them, `260704-pr0p` rework N4) stays centered in the grid; since `260714-uco1` it wraps an **inner anchor `<div className="flex items-center justify-start min-w-0 sm:min-w-[28ch]">`** ‚Äî a `sm:`-gated min-width with LEFT-aligned content so the heading's left edge stops drifting as the instance name length changes (below `sm` the min-width is absent ‚Äî space is scarce at 375px). The browser-history arrows + hierarchy ‚ñæ live INSIDE this anchored box (¬ß Center-heading stable anchor + nav affordances). It renders per mode:

- **terminal** (`mode === "terminal" && currentWindow`): `<HistoryNav>` ‚óÄ ‚ñ∂ + `<HierarchyDropdown mode="terminal">` (left of the prefix) + `<WindowHeading>` (static `Window: <window>`, editable name ‚Äî see ¬ß Window Heading) + the relocated bare-`‚ñæ` window switcher.
- **board** (`mode === "board" && boardName`): `<HistoryNav>` + `<HierarchyDropdown mode="board">` + a `<PageHeadingDisplay prefix="Board:" name={boardName}>` (display-only ‚Äî boards have no rename API) + the `<BoardSwitcher>` ‚ñæ (moved here from the left `BoardModeBreadcrumb`).
- **server** (`mode === "server" && server`): `<HistoryNav>` + `<HierarchyDropdown mode="server">` + `<PageHeadingDisplay prefix="tmux Server:" name={server}>` (display-only).
- **host**: `<HistoryNav>` + `<PageHeadingDisplay prefix="" name="Host" solo>` ‚Äî a solo type word, no instance name, primary-medium, visible at all breakpoints; NO hierarchy ‚ñæ (the root has no ancestors).

The type-prefix constants live once in `top-bar.tsx`: `WINDOW_PREFIX = "Window:"` (`260714-uco1`, replacing the retired `TERMINAL_PREFIX`/`terminalHeadingPrefix()`/`WEB_PREFIX`/`CHAT_PREFIX`), `BOARD_PREFIX = "Board:"`, `TMUX_SERVER_PREFIX = "tmux Server:"` (renamed from `CABIN_PREFIX = "Server Cabin:"` in `260715-zs1y`), `HOST_SOLO = "Host"` (renamed from `COCKPIT_SOLO = "Cockpit"` in `260715-zs1y`; title case, superseding PageHeading's lowercase idiom). Because the cell lives in the `auto` middle grid column, it stays centered under the topbar regardless of the breadcrumb / control-cluster widths. The `WindowHeading` (and the display headings) are deliberately NOT keyed on the route identity (no remount `key`) so they persist across window/page switches ‚Äî that is what lets the boot sweep replay on navigation and keeps an in-progress inline edit alive (an external windowId/server switch mid-edit CANCELS the stale edit instead, since committing the typed name onto the newly-navigated window would rename the wrong one ‚Äî the equivalent of the retired modal being pinned to the window it opened on).

### Center-heading stable anchor + nav affordances (`260714-uco1`)

Four affordances added to the top-bar center heading by `260714-uco1-topbar-heading-anchor-nav`, all inside the anchored center box (¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell), no new routes and no backend surface:

- **Stable left anchor.** The outer center cell stays `justify-center` in the grid; an INNER container `flex items-center justify-start min-w-0 sm:min-w-[28ch]` reserves a `sm:`-gated min-width with LEFT-aligned content, so the heading's left edge stops drifting as the instance name length changes (min-width chosen over fixed-width+truncate ‚Äî long names grow rightward, accepted). Applies uniformly across all four modes; below `sm` the min-width is absent (unchanged 375px behavior). The `28ch` value is monospace-exact (`Window: ` is 2ch shorter than the old `Terminal: `), visually tuned. The inline-rename `<input>` is `text-left` (was `text-center`) so the name does not jump on edit entry (¬ß Window Heading ‚Üí edit).
- **Hierarchy ‚ñæ dropdown** (`HierarchyDropdown`, reuses `BreadcrumbDropdown`). A bare-`‚ñæ` sibling of the rename button, bound LEFT of the prefix (reads `‚ñæ Window: name`), listing EXACTLY the current page's ANCESTOR chain ‚Äî no lateral jumps. Terminal: `tmux Server: {server}` (‚Üí `/{server}`) then `Host` (‚Üí `/`); board & server: `Host` only; **solo Host: not rendered** (the root has no ancestors). `hidden sm:inline-flex` ‚Äî below `sm` it rides with the hidden prefix span (the hamburger/sidebar covers mobile nav). Being a sibling of the rename button, clicking it never enters inline edit. Navigation routes through the typed `useNavigate()` (params validated). Known/accepted redundancy with the left breadcrumb (deferred ‚Äî out of scope).
- **Browser-history ‚óÄ ‚ñ∂ arrows** (`HistoryNav`). Fixed-width bordered `rk-glint` icon buttons (`coarse:` touch sizing, `aria-label`s) rendered LEFT of the prefix inside the anchored box on ALL FOUR modes (history is global). They call TanStack Router's `useRouter().history.back()` / `.forward()` ‚Äî BROWSER HISTORY, explicitly NOT sibling-window cycling. Being fixed-width they never shift the heading's text anchor. Forward is always-active (browser-chrome style ‚Äî `canGoForward` is not reliably exposed, so a dim/disabled state is best-effort and omitted; a no-forward click is a harmless no-op). **Within-server window hops retrace** since `260715-m4xy-history-push-window-switch`: user-initiated window switches now **push** history entries (`navigateToWindow` dropped its `replace: true` ‚Äî see ¬ß URL as Resumable Bookmark ‚Üí optimistic navigate), so Back/Forward step through every within-server hop, not only server boundaries. No dedup ‚Äî `w1‚Üíw5‚Üíw1` yields three entries. History Back/Forward bypasses `navigateToWindow` (raw `router.history.back()/forward()`), so no slide transition plays on arrow navigation; the landed window's tmux is realigned for free by the existing deep-link intent effect (¬ß URL as Resumable Bookmark, contract 1 ‚Äî its `hasAlignedToUrlRef` guard re-arms on every `windowParam` change).
- **`Go:` palette parity** (Constitution V) via the pure `lib/palette-nav.ts` builder `buildNavActions(mode, server, handlers)` (+ colocated `palette-nav.test.ts`), mirroring `palette-move.ts`/`palette-view.ts`. Returns the two history actions (`Go: Back`/`Go: Forward`, ALWAYS) followed by the route-appropriate ancestor entries (`Go: tmux Server` when `mode === "terminal" && server`; `Go: Host` for terminal/board/server). `app.tsx`'s `navActions` `useMemo` wires it into the `paletteActions` composition, passing `router.history.back/forward` + `navigate(...)` bodies, with `mode = windowParam ? "terminal" : "server"` ‚Äî AppShell never passes `"board"`/`"host"`, so the builder's `NavMode` `"board"`/`"host"` values have no production call site (plan-recorded deletion candidate: either wire `buildNavActions("board", ‚Ä¶)` into `boardRouteActions` or narrow the type). No new app-level keybindings (browser-native Alt+‚Üê/‚Üí already cover history).

**Board** (`/board/$name`, `mode="board"`): the left breadcrumb is brand + hamburger + a **counts/hint span ONLY** (`BoardModeInfo` ‚Äî `{N} pane[s] ¬∑ {M} server[s] ¬∑ ‚åò[‚åò] cycle`, no leading `‚Ä∫` because the hint is not a crumb). Since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` the board name + ‚ñæ switcher MOVED to the center heading (`Board: <board>` display + `<BoardSwitcher>`; ¬ß center cell), and the former left `Board ‚ñ∏` home button is GONE (the brand crumb is already the home affordance, and a left `Board` word would duplicate the centered type word ‚Äî move-don't-copy). This reduced the old `260702-6m46` `BoardModeBreadcrumb` (`Board ‚ñ∏ {name} ‚ñæ {counts}`) to just its counts/hint tail. Right cluster: the two L1 **SplitButtons** (wired to the focused tile's window via `focusedPane`, `260715-6jwn`) + the L2 controls (Aa + the board-only **autofit toggle** between Aa and ‚úï + ‚úï, where the board ‚úï is a **confirm-gated window-kill** of the focused tile's window since `260718-co9z` ‚Äî the ‚úï opens the kill dialog with a default-focused `Unpin instead` escape, ¬ß Board Kill Confirm Dialog; unpin lives on the tile-header pin-glyph + palette ‚Äî see ¬ß Right cluster / ¬ß Close pane button / ¬ß Board Tile Header / ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle) and the L3 always-block including the connection dot, which since `260704-9o7k` shows an **AND over the board's attached servers** (green iff ‚â•1 entry AND every distinct attached server's `isConnectedByServer` slice is connected; `board-page.tsx` derives `boardConnected` and passes it, replacing the old `isConnected={false}`). (Board mode no longer hides the dot ‚Äî the `260704-9o7k` change dropped that gate.)

**Mobile (`< sm`)** ‚Äî the brand collapses to the bare icon and intermediate crumbs (server link + session, plus their `‚Ä∫` separators, wrapped in `hidden sm:flex` spans) are hidden, leaving brand icon + the centered heading. Since `260704-pr0p` the leaf is the **center-cell heading in EVERY mode** (no longer just Terminal): Terminal ‚Üí `WindowHeading` (the mobile leaf AND primary rename affordance, `coarse:min-h-[30px]` touch target), tmux Server ‚Üí the `tmux Server: <server>` display heading, Board ‚Üí the `Board: <board>` display heading, Host ‚Üí the solo `Host`. **The two-tone `PageType:` prefix is hidden below `sm`** (`hidden sm:inline`) so mobile keeps just the name ‚Äî EXCEPT the solo `Host` word (a name-equivalent, not a prefix), which stays visible at all breakpoints. The `‚ñæ` window/board switcher stays visible on mobile with its `+ New Window` / board-switch action. Long names truncate in the center cell (`max-w-[16ch]` on mobile, `sm:max-w-[28ch]`) ‚Äî never wrap or squeeze neighbors. The topbar stays a single line at 375px (the documented invariant in `fab/project/context.md`).

**Mid-width overlap degradation (`260715-q8ey-top-bar-overlap-fixes`).** Between the `sm` breakpoint (640px) and ~900px, the bar's content used to fail as *unclipped overlap* ‚Äî the left breadcrumb text painted straight over the centered heading (garbled, unreadable) ‚Äî the primary run-kit use case of sidebars-open / half-screen browser panes. The fix installs a deterministic **degradation ladder** (a class-only edit to `top-bar.tsx`, no API/routing/backend change; the right cluster is deliberately untouched, see the deferred note):

1. **Crumbs truncate first.** The two left-nav crumb wrapper spans (server-link crumb + session crumb) each gained `min-w-0` so the `truncate max-w-[16ch]` already present on their inner anchor / `BreadcrumbDropdown` trigger finally engages. **`min-w-0`-chain rule**: a nested flex item defaults to `min-width: auto`, which blocks `truncate` from shrinking the item until an explicit `min-w-0` is added at that level ‚Äî the crumb text had been overflowing the nav box because the intervening wrapper span, not the anchor, was the blocked link in the chain. `BreadcrumbSeparator`, brand chip, and hamburger stay `shrink-0` ‚Äî the protected identity floor.
2. **Server crumb hides below `md`.** The server-link crumb wrapper was demoted `sm:`‚Üí`md:` (`hidden md:flex ‚Ä¶ min-w-0`) ‚Äî it is the natural first element to give way because the `260714-uco1` hierarchy ‚ñæ inside the heading prefix already lists `tmux Server: {server}` ‚Üí `Host`, so the left server crumb is redundant navigation at cramped widths. The **session crumb stays at `sm+`** (it owns the session switcher + `+ New Session` action).
3. **Nav clips at its explicit floor.** The `<nav aria-label="Breadcrumb">` dropped its bare `min-w-0` for an explicit breakpoint-aware floor `min-w-[76px] sm:min-w-[180px]` (below `sm` guarantees brand icon + hamburger ~76px; at `sm+` also a session-crumb sliver) plus `overflow-hidden`. **Clip-backstop rule**: `overflow-hidden` converts any residual overflow past the shrunk floor into a clean clip at the nav's right edge instead of paint-over overlap ‚Äî overlap becomes structurally impossible, not merely unlikely. The `min-w-[76px] sm:min-w-[180px]` starting values held across the full Playwright sweep (375 / 640 / 700 / 768 / 1024px) with no adjustment needed ‚Äî they are the final tuned values. (A clipped child keeps a layout box wider than its clipping parent, which is expected; the meaningful proofs are the no-intersection assertion + computed `overflow:hidden`, not a layout-box comparison.)

**Center protection (`260715-q8ey`).** The center `auto` grid column is protected by holding its bounded **content floor**, NOT by a magic pixel min-width. The fix **removed `min-w-0` from the center cell's OUTER wrapper** (`flex items-center justify-center`) so the `auto` column can no longer be squeezed below the heading's content.
