That floor is *bounded* (cannot grow unbounded) because the heading name spans carry `max-w-[16ch] sm:max-w-[28ch] truncate` (WindowHeading button + PageHeadingDisplay) and the history ‚óÄ ‚ñ∂ / hierarchy ‚ñæ / window & board ‚ñæ controls are fixed-width `shrink-0`. The inner box's **`sm:min-w-[28ch]` stable anchor stays at `sm:` (deliberately NOT demoted to `md:`)** ‚Äî an earlier "demote the anchor" idea was superseded once the companion overflow-chevron change makes the *right* cluster absorb squeeze. Net effect: squeeze lands on the left (and right) `1fr` columns; the center heading is never compressed into overlap across the 640‚Äì900px band.

**Right-cluster degradation (`260715-q8ey` deferred ‚Üí `260715-h1ck` shipped).** `q8ey` added NO `min-w-0`/`overflow-hidden` to the right cluster and left its degradation to the companion overflow-chevron change. **`260715-h1ck-top-bar-overflow-chevron-menu` now ships that degradation**: the right cluster is registry-driven and its `1fr` grid track is made squeezable via `min-w-0` on the cell, so under width pressure controls collapse into a chevron menu instead of clipping (full mechanics in ¬ß Right cluster ‚Üí overflow chevron menu below). `q8ey`'s note that a partial `overflow-hidden` on the right cluster would clip the *wrong* end (flex overflow spills toward inline-end, dropping the L3 always-block / connection dot first) is why `h1ck` uses an explicit fit computation + move-to-menu instead of `overflow-hidden` ‚Äî and why the `h1ck` cell carries `min-w-0` but deliberately NO `overflow-hidden` (the only content that can exceed a very-narrow track is the always-present exempt chevron+dot block, which must stay visible/clickable per R6). Regression coverage lives in `tests/e2e/top-bar-overlap.spec.ts` (+ `.spec.md`): at ~700√ó800 with long window + session names, nav-box ‚à© heading-box is empty and crumbs are ellipsised; server crumb toggles across `md`; 375px stays single-line; 1024px+ keeps the anchor intact. The `h1ck` width-sweep spec `tests/e2e/top-bar-overflow.spec.ts` (+ `.spec.md`) is the right-cluster's own regression proof (see ¬ß Right cluster).

**Right cluster** (`flex items-center justify-end gap-3 min-w-0`, since `260715-h1ck`; was `justify-self-end` pre-`h1ck`) ‚Äî a **strict 3-level cumulative pyramid** (`260704-9o7k-top-bar-button-pyramid`), growing LEFTWARD from a stable always-block pinned right, so no shared button ever changes screen position between pages. **Since `260715-h1ck-top-bar-overflow-chevron-menu` the pyramid is consumed by a priority+ overflow menu** (¬ß Right cluster ‚Üí overflow chevron menu below): the same L1‚ÜíL2‚ÜíL3 order now encodes DROP priority (L1 drops first, L3 last) and the whole cluster is registry-driven, not hardcoded JSX. The tiers:

| Level | Gate | Buttons (left ‚Üí right) |
|---|---|---|
| **L1** ‚Äî splits terminal+board, FixedWidthToggle terminal-only (`260715-6jwn`) | splits: `currentWindow` (terminal) OR `mode === "board" && focusedPane` (board); FixedWidthToggle: `mode === "terminal"` | SplitButton (vertical) ¬∑ SplitButton (horizontal) ¬∑ **FixedWidthToggle (terminal-only)** |
| **L2** ‚Äî terminal + board | `mode === "terminal" \|\| mode === "board"` | TerminalFontControl (Aa) ¬∑ **BoardAutofitToggle (board-only, between Aa and ‚úï)** ¬∑ **ClosePaneButton (‚úï ‚Äî terminal: close-pane; board: confirm-gated window-kill via `onRequestKill`, `260718-co9z`)** |
| **L3** ‚Äî always (all four modes) | none | **UpdateChip (‚¨Ü v‚Ä¶ ‚Äî leading, conditional: hidden unless a qualifying, un-dismissed, non-dev update is pending ‚Äî `260713-4zap`)** ¬∑ NotificationControl (üîî) ¬∑ ThemeToggle (‚óê) ¬∑ **RefreshButton (‚ü≥)** ¬∑ HelpLink (?) ¬∑ **connection dot (‚óè)** |

Each control carries the shared `rk-glint` chip styling (`min-w-[24px] min-h-[24px] coarse:min-w-[30px] coarse:min-h-[30px]`). **The former per-control `hidden sm:flex` breakpoint cliff (the whole cluster was desktop-only ‚Äî mobile hid it) is GONE since `260715-h1ck`**: controls no longer vanish below `sm`; under width pressure they overflow into the chevron menu at any width (¬ß Right cluster ‚Üí overflow chevron menu). L1's absence on non-terminal pages just widens the gap to the breadcrumb; the L3 always-block keeps its fixed right edge (the brand anchor moved to the left nav as the root crumb ‚Äî `260702-6m46`). Deltas `260704-9o7k` introduced from the prior "mostly mode-invariant" cluster:

- **L3 order is user-specified**: Notification ‚Üí Theme ‚Üí Refresh ‚Üí Help, then the dot as the **right-most status terminator** (not a button). Since `260713-4zap` the conditional **UpdateChip leads the block** (Update ‚Üí Notification ‚Üí Theme ‚Üí Refresh ‚Üí Help ‚Üí dot) ‚Äî it renders only when a qualifying, un-dismissed, non-`dev` update is pending, so its absence just tightens the gap (¬ß Update Notification).
- **RefreshButton promoted** L1 ‚Üí L3 (was terminal-only; now renders in every mode ‚Äî a reload is meaningful everywhere; behavior unchanged: plain click `window.location.reload()`, Shift+click `forceReload()`). See ¬ß Refresh button.
- **FixedWidthToggle demoted** always ‚Üí L1 (now terminal-only). Its *behavior* is untouched: the 900px `maxWidth` wrapper lives in AppShell (`app.tsx`), which renders both `terminal` AND `server`, so **the tmux Server page keeps the constraint and the `View: Fixed Width` palette access** ‚Äî only the tmux Server page button is removed (it was already a no-op on Board/Host, which never read `fixedWidth`). See ¬ß Command Palette View actions.
- **TerminalFontControl (Aa)** gating simplified from `mode !== "server" && mode !== "host"` to the L2 predicate `mode === "terminal" || mode === "board"` (same effective result ‚Äî a terminal-bearing surface: the single window or a board pane).
- **ClosePaneButton (‚úï) is mode-branched** (one component): terminal ‚úï is a real close-pane (`closePane`) of the current window's active pane; board ‚úï (since `260718-co9z`) routes through `onRequestKill` to open the **kill confirm dialog** whose confirmed action is a window-kill of the focused tile's window (`260715-6jwn` had made board ‚úï a direct `closePane`; `260718-co9z` gates it and escalates it to a window-kill with an `Unpin instead` escape). Unpin lives on the tile header + palette, not the ‚úï. See ¬ß Close pane button / ¬ß Board Kill Confirm Dialog.
- **BoardAutofitToggle is board-only, INSIDE L2** (`260708-738w`): a new toggle rendered **between Aa and ‚úï** in the L2 cluster, but gated `mode === "board" && onToggleAutofit` (narrower than the L2 predicate ‚Äî it does NOT appear on terminal). Mirrors `FixedWidthToggle` (`aria-pressed`, `rk-glint`, `coarse:` sizing) and flips the per-board desktop autofit preference. See ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle.

**Overflow chevron menu (priority+ degradation, `260715-h1ck-top-bar-overflow-chevron-menu`).** The pyramid above is now consumed by a browser-toolbar-style priority+ overflow menu: as the right `1fr` track shrinks, controls drop into a dropdown behind an always-visible down-chevron rather than clipping (the `q8ey` interim behavior) or vanishing (the retired `hidden sm:flex` cliff). Registry + measurement live in `top-bar.tsx`; the chevron/menu component is `components/top-bar-overflow-menu.tsx`; the fit math is `lib/top-bar-overflow.ts` (+ colocated `.test.ts`).

- **Ordered registry replaces the hardcoded JSX.** The right cluster is built from an ordered `RegistryEntry[]` (`{ id, tier ‚Äî implicit in position, modes: TopBarMode[], hidden?, barRender: () => ReactNode, menuRender: () => ReactNode }`), one entry per control in drop order ‚Äî **`view-switcher` LEADS the list since `260717-6anu`** (terminal-only, first-to-drop), then the pyramid: L1 split-vertical ¬∑ split-horizontal ¬∑ fixed-width; L2 terminal-font ¬∑ autofit ¬∑ close-pane; L3 update-chip ¬∑ notification ¬∑ theme ¬∑ refresh ¬∑ help. One ordered source drives BOTH the bar (first-that-fit render `barRender` as icon buttons) and the menu (the rest render `menuRender` as labeled rows), so bar‚Üîmenu can never drift. Filtered per render by `modes.includes(mode)` and the optional `hidden` predicate (an entry with `hidden` true renders NOWHERE ‚Äî not bar, not menu, not the measurement probe): `view-switcher` `hidden: !(mode==="terminal" && currentWindow && onSelectView && availableViews && availableViews.length > 1)` (the negation of the full render gate, so a tty-only / single-view window contributes no bar slot, menu row, or probe width ‚Äî `260717-6anu`); `notification` `hidden: pushUnsupported`; splits/fixed-width `hidden: !currentWindow`; autofit `hidden: !(mode==="board" && onToggleAutofit)`; `update-chip` `hidden: !showChip` (kept out of the candidate set entirely so it never reserves an empty slot). This **kills the per-item `hidden sm:flex` empty-flex-item gap hack** UpdateChip and NotificationControl used to self-carry ‚Äî gating is now 100% registry data.

- **Drop order = registry consumed from the LEFT; surviving buttons never shift.** Overflow eats the **`view-switcher` FIRST** (since `260717-6anu` ‚Äî it leads the list), then L1, then L2, then L3, leftmost-within-tier first ‚Äî so the surviving in-bar set is a SUFFIX of the registry order and every survivor keeps its exact screen position (the pyramid invariant, preserved; the pill keeps its leftmost in-bar position while it survives). Implementation: the fit function reverses the measured widths (L3-end first), `computeVisibleCount` greedily fits from the tail, and the returned N trailing candidates stay in-bar while the leading `candidates.length ‚àí N` overflow into the menu (in registry order). `visibleItems = candidates.slice(splitAt)`, `overflowItems = candidates.slice(0, splitAt)`. `computeVisibleCount`/`lib/top-bar-overflow.ts` is UNTOUCHED ‚Äî adding the view-switcher as the first candidate needed no fit-math change (the suffix invariant already handles a longer candidate list).

- **Exempt items never overflow**: since `260717-6anu` the exempt set is only the **overflow chevron itself** and the **connection dot** ‚Äî the ViewSwitcher LEFT the exempt set and is now the first *candidate* (¬ß ViewSwitcher chip; it drops first, before L1). The chevron+dot render in a **trailing block** (`trailingRef`, chevron immediately LEFT of the dot ‚Äî the dot keeps its right-most status-terminator role); their measured width is the only thing RESERVED before candidates are placed. So `reserved = trailing + RIGHT_GAP_PX` (the trailing block plus one `gap-3` joining it to the last candidate) ‚Äî the former `+ (vsw > 0 ? vsw + gap : 0)` ViewSwitcher-reservation term, the `viewSwitcherRef`, and its `ro.observe` line were all REMOVED; the pill's width is now contributed by the probe row like every other candidate.

- **Attention badge**: when an attention-bearing item is overflowed ‚Äî today only the UpdateChip, i.e. `showChip && overflowItems` contains `update-chip` (`updateOverflowed`) ‚Äî the chevron carries a small accent-green dot so the update signal isn't lost when the chip is hidden into the menu. No badge when the chip is in-bar or no qualifying update.

- **Always-present menu + fixed version row.** The chevron renders even when nothing overflows, because the menu ALWAYS ends with a fixed `Run Kit v{version}` row (¬ß Steady-state version surfaces ‚Üí surface 5): click copies the displayed version + toasts; plain `Run Kit` when `daemonVersion` is null. When a qualifying update is pending AND the UpdateChip is overflowed, that row FLIPS to the update surface (`Run Kit v{current} ‚Üí v{latest} ‚¨Ü`, click = `updateNow()`) and no separate UpdateChip menu row is added (the `update-chip` entry's `menuRender` returns `null` by design). The chip and the version-row update surface share the `useUpdateClick()` hook so the updating-state + failure toast can't drift.

- **Menu-row representations** (`menuRender` closures): view-switcher ‚Üí **one `View: {label}` row per available view** (`View: Terminal`/`View: Web`/`View: Chat`) via `ViewSwitcherMenuRows` in tty-first `orderViews()` order, active row inverse-video accent-green + `aria-pressed`, click = `onSelectView(view)` + close (`260717-6anu`, ¬ß ViewSwitcher chip ‚Üí overflow representation); splits ‚Üí "Split vertical" / "Split horizontal"; fixed-width ‚Üí "Fixed width" `role="menuitemcheckbox"` (checked=`fixedWidth`); terminal-font (Aa) ‚Üí an inline `‚àí`/`+` stepper `role="group"` row operating on `terminalFontSize` within `TERMINAL_FONT_BOUNDS` (does NOT reopen the Aa popover); autofit ‚Üí "Autofit panes" checkbox row; close-pane ‚Üí "Close pane" in BOTH modes (real close-pane since `260715-6jwn` ‚Äî no longer the board "Unpin pane" label) honoring the same disabled conditions; notification ‚Üí NotificationControl's own dropdown FLATTENED into direct "Enable notifications" / "Send test notification" rows; theme ‚Üí "Theme: {current}" cycle row (shares the extracted `cycleTheme()` with the in-bar ThemeToggle ‚Äî review M5); refresh ‚Üí "Refresh page" row (Shift+click force-reload preserved; the "page" word disambiguates from the `Status: Refresh` palette action, `260715-jykd`); help ‚Üí "Help / Documentation" external `HELP_URL` link.

- **Menu a11y mirrors `BreadcrumbDropdown`**: `role="menu"` panel / `role="menuitem"`/`menuitemcheckbox` rows, `position: fixed` anchored to the trigger rect (top just below, right-aligned ‚Äî no ancestor `overflow-hidden` clips it, no new dependency), Escape closes + refocuses the chevron, ArrowUp/ArrowDown move focus, outside `mousedown` closes, glued to a moving trigger via scroll/resize reflow. **Row-click close keys on the target's ROLE, not the row wrapper** (review S1): a click landing on a `role="menuitem"`/`menuitemcheckbox` closes the panel (single-shot action), but the font stepper's `‚àí`/`+` are plain buttons inside a `role="group"`, so repeated stepping does NOT close the menu.

- **Measurement mechanism** (in `top-bar.tsx`, collapse-first, no hysteresis): the right cell is given `min-w-0` so its `1fr` grid track is squeezable (relies on `q8ey`'s left/center floors, so the track width is grid-determined ‚Äî no feedback loop, no oscillation). **The cell must FILL the `1fr` track ‚Äî `flex ‚Ä¶ justify-end ‚Ä¶ min-w-0`, NOT `justify-self-end`** (M1, load-bearing): `justify-self-end` content-sizes the box, which both deadlocks the fit (with collapse-first `visibleCount=0` the box measures only the exempt block ‚Üí budget < 0 forever) and never fires the ResizeObserver on window resize (a content-sized box's width doesn't track the viewport); default grid stretch fills the track and `justify-end` right-aligns content inside it. A single `ResizeObserver` observes the cell + a hidden off-screen `inert`/`aria-hidden` **probe row** (renders every candidate's `barRender` so real widths are always known ‚Äî buttons vary by ViewSwitcher/UpdateChip/`coarse:` sizing, nothing hardcoded; since `260717-6anu` the ViewSwitcher is a candidate IN this probe row, no longer a separately-observed exempt node) + the trailing chevron/dot block (the only reserved node now), so reserved/candidate width changes (the ViewSwitcher's probe width changing when it gains a segment or the active segment shifts, the UpdateChip's `‚¨Ü v{latest}` label width changing) re-fit too even though they don't resize the outer cell (S2). The measure effect's dep array retains `availableViews`/`activeView` because the ViewSwitcher's probe width still varies with segment count and the active segment. The pure `computeVisibleCount(availableWidth, itemWidths, reservedWidth, gap)` (front-consuming greedy fit, `gap` charged between rendered items only, clamp `[0, len]`, 0 for a non-positive budget) is unit-tested in isolation. Collapse-first: `visibleCount` starts at 0 (`useState(0)`) and is set in a `useLayoutEffect` before paint, so no flash of overflowing buttons. The cell carries `min-w-0` but deliberately **NO `overflow-hidden`** ‚Äî the only content that can exceed a very-narrow track is the always-present exempt chevron+dot block, which must stay visible/clickable (R6); `.app-shell`/`header` still clip any horizontal page overflow.

- **Keyboard path unchanged (Constitution V)**: the menu is a pointer affordance; the command palette already exposes every affected action, so no palette changes were needed (the menu is itself keyboard-operable per its a11y contract). Coverage: `lib/top-bar-overflow.test.ts` (fit edge cases ‚Äî untouched by `260717-6anu`), `top-bar.test.tsx` / `update-chip.test.tsx` (chevron presence, menu open, version-row states, a working menu action), `view-switcher.test.tsx` (the `ViewSwitcherMenuRows` per-view rows in `orderViews()` order, active marking + aria, click callback, single-view `null`), and the width-sweep e2e `tests/e2e/top-bar-overflow.spec.ts` (+ `.spec.md`) ‚Äî 1280‚Üí‚Ä¶‚Üí375px asserting no overlap, monotonic drop, menu = exactly the dropped controls + version row, exempt items always visible, and a menu action firing; since `260717-6anu` extended on a multi-view window to prove the view-switcher is FIRST-to-drop (overflows before any L1 split) with its per-view `View:` menu rows + row activation switching the lens (the tty-only `WINDOW_NAME` window has no view-switcher candidate, so the existing pyramid sweep is unaffected). The e2e is the regression proof for the M1 fit-wiring fix (jsdom's zero widths mean the Vitest layer can't catch fit defects).

**Connection dot** (`role="status"`, `aria-live="polite"`, green `bg-accent-green` / gray `bg-text-secondary`, `aria-label` Connected/Disconnected) ‚Äî the right-most element, now in **ALL four modes** (`260704-9o7k` dropped the former `mode !== "board" && mode !== "host"` gate). Since `260715-ifco-expose-running-version-ui` it also carries a hover **`title`** that folds in the running version ‚Äî a computed `dotTitle`: `Disconnected` when `!isConnected`, else `Connected ‚Äî run-kit {displayVersion(daemonVersion)}` when `daemonVersion` is known, else bare `Connected` (the version fragment is OMITTED until the first `version` event so the title is never `vundefined`). `daemonVersion` is read via `useUpdateNotification()` (already imported for the UpdateChip); `displayVersion` from `lib/palette-version`. The **`aria-label` stays the concise `Connected`/`Disconnected`** ‚Äî the version is hover-discovery detail, not screen-reader-essential state on the live region. Its meaning is per-page "this page's live data is flowing", derived by each caller and passed as `isConnected`.

**Since `260716-qf3j-state-socket` a dot reads Connected only when the state socket is connected AND the page's relevant subscription has ACKED** (was "the SSE stream is open"). The two-part gate is the whole delta: a bare socket connection is not enough ‚Äî the subscription must have received its `ack` (the fresh snapshot), which is the WS analogue of the pre-change "first sessions event". Per-caller derivation:

- **Terminal / tmux Server**: the current server's slice `isConnected` (`isConnectedByServer.get(server)` mirrored through ChromeProvider) ‚Äî now true iff the socket is up AND that server's `subscribe` acked (its slice flips Connected on `ack`, and back on the socket-level disconnect debounce). Reconnect nuance (nice-to-have, `A-011`): on socket re-open a previously-acked server flips Connected before its fresh re-ack lands (ms-scale window).
- **Host**: `hostMetricsConnected` from `useSessionContext()` ‚Äî the dedicated `metrics` subscription's debounced ack-health when no server is attached, else true iff any attached server subscription is connected (per-server metrics fan-out); architecture.md ¬ß Server-independent host-metrics subscription.
- **Board**: `boardConnected` ‚Äî AND over the board's attached servers (green iff ‚â•1 entry AND every distinct attached server's slice is connected, i.e. subscribed-and-acked).

**Help link** (`HelpLink` in `top-bar.tsx`; `260704-hmd0-help-icon-top-bar`): an external-docs chip in the L3 always-block, after `RefreshButton` (since `260704-9o7k` inserted Refresh between Theme and Help) and before the connection dot. Since `260715-h1ck` it is a registry candidate (`id: "help"`), not `hidden sm:flex`-wrapped ‚Äî it overflows into the chevron menu as a "Help / Documentation" row when it doesn't fit. An **`<a>`, not a button** ‚Äî it navigates externally to the exported `HELP_URL` constant (`https://shll.ai/run-kit`) with `target="_blank"` + `rel="noopener noreferrer"`, so the live dashboard (terminals, SSE) is never unloaded. Carries the shared cluster chip styling verbatim (`rk-glint` glint hover + `min-w-[24px] min-h-[24px] coarse:min-w-[30px] coarse:min-h-[30px] rounded border border-border text-text-secondary hover:border-text-secondary`) and a 14px inline `currentColor` `?` SVG glyph matching the sibling icons; `aria-label`/`title` "Help ‚Äî run-kit docs". `HELP_URL` is defined once in `top-bar.tsx` (mirroring the `NOTIFICATIONS_HELP_URL` precedent) and **exported** so the palette action reuses the same constant ‚Äî the two cannot drift. The palette counterpart is the `Help: Documentation` action (`id: "help-documentation"`), registered in `app.tsx`'s `configActions` next to `Help: Keyboard Shortcuts` ‚Äî so it reaches the **AppShell palette only** (Terminal + tmux Server), NOT the board route's own `boardRouteActions` (which carries only `refresh-page` + the terminal-font trio) and NOT the Host page (mounts no palette). **The chip itself renders on every route** (mode-invariant right cluster); it is only the *palette* affordance that is AppShell-scoped. Unit-tested in `top-bar.test.tsx` (asserts `href`, `target="_blank"`, `rel` containing `noopener`, and an accessible name); no dedicated e2e ‚Äî a static anchor in existing chrome has no interactive flow to drive.

**Split buttons** (`SplitButton` in `top-bar.tsx`): Two inline components calling `splitWindow(server, windowId, horizontal, cwd)` from `api/client.ts`. Custom SVG icons (square-split pattern). Best-effort error handling ‚Äî tmux may reject if pane is too small. `POST /api/windows/{windowId}/split` with `{ "horizontal": bool }`. **Rendered on terminal AND board mode since `260715-6jwn`** (L1). Terminal: `server`/`windowId` come from `currentWindow`, `server` read from `useSessionContext()`. Board: fed by the slot's `focusedPane` ‚Äî a `mode === "board" && focusedPane && (...)` block renders the same two `SplitButton`s wired to the **focused tile's** `{server, windowId, cwd}`. Window IDs are server-unique, so targeting a pinned window's ID works even though it lives in a hidden `_rk-pin-*` session; the split lands relative to that window's active pane and renders live inside the tile. Absent when the board is empty (no `focusedPane`); same `hidden sm:flex` gating as terminal (no mobile change).

**Close pane button** (`ClosePaneButton` in `top-bar.tsx`): the L2 ‚úï chip ‚Äî **mode-branched** between a terminal close-pane and a board window-kill. Props: `server?`, `windowId?`, `disabled?: boolean`, `onClosed?: () => void`, `onRequestKill?: () => void` (board routing, `260718-co9z`), `label = "Close pane"`.
- **Terminal mode**: the optimistic close-pane path ‚Äî `closePane(server, windowId)` via `useOptimisticAction`, spinner (`LogoSpinner`) + `disabled` while `isPending`. `POST /api/windows/{windowId}/close-pane` ‚Üí `tmux.KillActivePane`. Rendered only when `currentWindow` exists; also "Pane: Close" in the palette. Terminal-mode ‚úï semantics are UNCHANGED (out of scope of `260718-co9z`).
- **Board mode**: when `onRequestKill` is present (registered by `BoardPage`, `260718-co9z`) the ‚úï calls it INSTEAD of `closePane`, opening the **kill confirm dialog** (¬ß Board Kill Confirm Dialog) rather than firing immediately; the confirmed action is a window-kill (`killWindow`), not a close-pane, with an `Unpin instead` escape. Its label/aria/tooltip become "Kill". `disabled={!focusedPane}` so the ‚úï is disabled on an empty board. (`260715-6jwn` had made board ‚úï a direct unconfirmed `closePane`; `260718-co9z` gates + escalates it because a board pane's blast radius ‚Äî the whole window everywhere, including its home session ‚Äî was illegible.)
- **`onClosed` self-heal seam**: post-kill board refetch no longer rides an `onClosed` callback on this button ‚Äî it rides `executeKillWindow`'s own `onSettled` in `board-page.tsx` (¬ß Board Kill Confirm Dialog). The dead direct-kill `onPaneClosed` slot seam is removed. (The self-heal still covers the no-`board-changed`-on-kill gap: killing a window collapses its single-window pin-session with no `board-changed` SSE event ‚Äî fired only by pin/unpin/reorder ‚Äî so the refetch lets `getBoard` drop the vanished tile and an emptied board fall out of `GET /api/boards`.)

X-shaped close icon SVG (`width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24"`), shared `rk-glint` chip styling. Since `260715-h1ck` it is the L2 registry `close-pane` candidate (no longer `hidden sm:flex`-wrapped) ‚Äî it renders in-bar when it fits and overflows into the chevron menu as a "Close pane" (terminal) / "Kill" (board) row honoring the same disabled conditions (board `disabled={!focusedPane}`). Unpin is not on the ‚úï ‚Äî it survives only as the tile-header pin-glyph button (¬ß Board Tile Header) and the `Board: Unpin Focused Pane` palette action (¬ß Boards Command Palette), both driven by the shared `unpinFocused` handler in `board-page.tsx` (`unpin(entries[focusedIndex].server, .windowId, name)`, `POST /api/boards/{name}/unpin`).

**Board autofit toggle** (`BoardAutofitToggle` in `top-bar.tsx`; `260708-738w-board-autofit`): the L2 cluster's **board-only** toggle, rendered **between `Aa` (`TerminalFontControl`) and `‚úï` (`ClosePaneButton`)** but gated on `mode === "board" && onToggleAutofit` (narrower than the terminal+board L2 predicate ‚Äî it never renders on the Terminal route). Props: `autofit: boolean`, `onToggle: () => void`. Mirrors the `FixedWidthToggle` vocabulary ‚Äî `aria-label="Toggle board autofit"`, `aria-pressed={autofit}`, shared `rk-glint` glint hover + `coarse:` touch sizing, `title` reflecting on/off ("Autofit on (panes fill the row)" / "Autofit off (fixed pane widths)"). Clicking it flips the per-board desktop autofit preference; the palette counterpart `Board: Toggle Autofit (on/off)` flips the SAME state (Constitution V parity). It is wired from `BoardPage` through the top-bar slot context (`autofit` + `onToggleAutofit`) ‚Üí `RootTopBar` (`app.tsx`) ‚Üí `TopBar` props (tolerant-empty: absent `onToggleAutofit` ‚áí no toggle). The behavior it controls (equal-share flex layout, hidden resize handles, non-destructive stored-width round-trip) lives in ¬ß Board Autofit Toggle.

**Refresh button** (`RefreshButton` in `top-bar.tsx`; `260703-p29w-topbar-refresh-button`): part of the **L3 always-block since `260704-9o7k`** ‚Äî promoted out of the former terminal-only group into the always-block (a reload is meaningful on every page), rendered between `ThemeToggle` and `HelpLink` (was Terminal-only, immediately after `ClosePaneButton` inside the `currentWindow &&` block, pre-`9o7k`). **Since `260715-h1ck` it is a registry candidate** (`id: "refresh"`), no longer wrapped in a `hidden sm:flex` span ‚Äî it renders in-bar in all four modes when it fits and overflows into the chevron menu as a "Refresh page" row otherwise (reachable below `sm` where it previously vanished). Its behavior is **byte-for-byte unchanged** by the move. A **plain `<button type="button">`** whose `onClick` does a **full page reload** ‚Äî plain click `window.location.reload()`; **Shift+click force-reloads** via the exported `forceReload()` helper (a `fetch(location.href, { cache: "reload" })` that overwrites the document's HTTP cache entry, then `reload()` in `.finally` so it fires even offline ‚Äî Chrome Shift+reload semantics; the legacy `reload(true)` forceGet flag is dead in modern browsers. The fetch races a 3s timeout (`Promise.race`, then `clearTimeout` in `.finally`) so a **stalled** socket that never resolves *or* rejects still reloads ‚Äî `.catch` alone covers rejection but not an indefinite hang). `aria-label` "Refresh page", `title` "Refresh page (Shift+click: force reload)", carrying the shared cluster className (`min-w-[24px] min-h-[24px] coarse:min-w-[30px] coarse:min-h-[30px] rounded border border-border ‚Ä¶`) and a 14√ó14 `aria-hidden` stroke SVG (lucide `rotate-cw` ‚Äî a circular arrow + top-right arrowhead, `stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2"`, round caps/joins) matching the sibling split/close glyphs. It is the in-app recovery affordance for degraded terminal views (stale relay / wedged xterm / SSE drift) where browser chrome is out of reach (PWA/standalone/kiosk). Deliberately **NO spinner / `useOptimisticAction` / `isPending` / `LogoSpinner`, NO `disabled` state, and NO confirmation** (unlike Split / Close) ‚Äî the page unloads synchronously so a spinner would never meaningfully render, and the reload is non-destructive by design (constitution II/VI: all client state re-derives on load; tmux sessions are unaffected). The same action is also reachable from the command palette as "View: Refresh Page" (see ¬ß Boards Command Palette / ¬ß Command Palette View actions below). *(Rejected during intake: a `TerminalClient` `key`-bump remount to reconnect just the relay ‚Äî deferred as a possible follow-up; tmux `respawn-pane` ‚Äî destructive, kills the running process.)*

**Toolbar button color convention**: All toolbar buttons (top bar and bottom bar) use `text-text-secondary` as their default foreground color. Active toggle states (Ctrl/Alt modifiers when armed, FixedWidthToggle when active) use `text-accent` with accent background. Hover state uses `hover:border-text-secondary` (border highlight). This convention applies to: compose button, theme toggle, fixed-width toggle, split buttons, close pane button, Esc, Tab, Ctrl, Alt, Fn trigger, arrow pad, and ‚åòK.

### Window Heading (`WindowHeading` in `top-bar.tsx`, `260703-5ilm`)

The centered, highlighted, editable window heading ‚Äî the single most important identity on the Terminal route (the tmux window name, e.g. `riff-gallant-jackal`). It gives the window name the prominence of a document title (mental model: browser-tab / editor title bar) and makes rename lowest-friction direct manipulation. Lives in the top bar's center grid cell (¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell); renders only when `mode === "terminal" && currentWindow`. Since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` it is the terminal instance of the universal `PageType: name` heading ‚Äî a static prefix span sits OUTSIDE the rename button, and the name is driven by the shared boot-sweep primitive (`useBootSweep`/`SweepCells`, ¬ß Hover-Animation Vocabulary ‚Üí boot sweep) that replaced the standalone decode scramble. **The prefix is a static `Window:` in every lens** (¬ß Heading is a static `Window:`; `260714-uco1` spec-R4 reversal): `WindowHeading` takes a `prefix` prop, but the sole call site now passes the CONSTANT `WINDOW_PREFIX` ‚Äî the lens-following `terminalHeadingPrefix()` + `WEB_PREFIX`/`CHAT_PREFIX` were retired, and the heading no longer varies by lens (the `ViewSwitcher` shows the lens ‚Äî the overflow-registry chip or, when collapsed, its `View:` menu rows, `260717-6anu`). The boot-sweep + inline-rename are carried over unchanged. (History: `260714-r7rq` first parametrized the prefix and `260714-t97o-web-view-lens` generalized it to the lens machinery; `260714-uco1` reverted it to a constant. The `prevPrefixRef` + prefix-keyed replay effect that a lens flip once drove is now INERT ‚Äî a constant prefix can never change ‚Äî and survives only as a plan-recorded deletion candidate.)

**Two-tone prefix** (`260704-pr0p`): the `Window:` prefix (static in every lens since `260714-uco1`) renders `text-text-secondary` as a **static sibling span outside the rename button/input** (`hidden sm:inline` ‚Äî mobile keeps just the name) ‚Äî clicking it never starts an edit, and the button's `aria-label` stays clean. The name keeps `font-semibold text-text-primary`. The prefix's frame states (dim ahead of cursor / typed behind) come from the boot sweep's `prefix` half.

**Three states** (one component):

- **display** ‚Äî a `<button aria-label="Rename window {name}" title="Click to rename">` rendering the name (via `<SweepCells>` at rest ‚Üí plain text) at `text-sm font-semibold text-text-primary` (weight-600 + primary color IS the "highlighted" rest state; the surrounding crumbs are secondary, so weight+color alone read as highlighted ‚Äî no background). `max-w-[16ch] sm:max-w-[28ch] inline-flex items-center coarse:min-h-[30px]` (mobile-leaf touch target), with the name inside an inner `min-w-0 truncate` span ‚Äî truncation MUST live on the span, not the button: `text-overflow` is inert on a flex container, and flex centering clipped long names on BOTH ends with no ellipsis (`riff-blustery-whale` ‚Üí `iff-blustery-whal`). Left-anchored, so long names keep their head and cut at the tail; the button itself stays centered in the grid cell. Click enters edit.
- **boot sweep** (was "decode") ‚Äî the JS sweep from `useBootSweep` (¬ß Hover-Animation Vocabulary ‚Üí boot sweep). One inverse-video accent-green cursor at `DECODE_FRAME_MS = 28`ms/cell sweeps `Window:` + space + name; over the prefix it types (TypedLabel states), over the name it churns `DECODE_GLYPHS`. Crucially the heading container NO LONGER flips `text-accent-green` for the whole scramble (`260704-pr0p` rework M2/N2) ‚Äî green lives ONLY on the per-cell churn/cursor spans inside `SweepCells`; each resolved cell settles to its own REST color (`restCellClass`: prefix ‚Üí `text-secondary`, name ‚Üí semibold `text-primary`), so the left-to-right two-tone reveal is visible instead of a uniform green flash. **Guards** (intake A5, all preserved): (a) a `DECODE_HOVER_INTENT_MS = 140`ms hover-intent delay before the sweep starts (cursor transit toward the right buttons doesn't replay it); (b) edit-start stops the sweep and the input binds to the real `name`/`draft` state, never the scrambled DOM text; (c) the sweep replays once whenever the **DISPLAYED name changes** ‚Äî a `prevNameRef` **seeded `null`** effect keyed on the incoming `name` prop. The null seed is the `260704-pr0p` mount-replay fix (rework M1): the sweep plays ONCE on mount (first name resolution flips `prevNameRef` from `null`), so route navigation between page types animates ‚Äî AND a committed rename, an SSE external rename, and window navigation all still replay through the same name-change mechanism (this is why the instance is NOT remounted per window ‚Äî a fresh mount re-seeds `prevNameRef` to `null` and would replay every time / double-play). Skipped entirely under `prefers-reduced-motion` (`prefersReducedMotion()` reads `window.matchMedia`, guarded for jsdom ‚Äî the rest state IS the reduced-motion state).
- **edit** ‚Äî an identically-styled inline `<input aria-label="Window name">` (monospace, `text-left font-semibold text-text-primary`, `border-b border-accent`; `text-left` since `260714-uco1` ‚Äî dropped `text-center` so the name does not jump horizontally on edit entry now that the heading is left-anchored), width sized in `ch` and growing with content (`Math.max(draft.length + 1, 3)ch`), `autoFocus` + select-on-focus. **Enter commits, Escape cancels, blur commits**; empty/whitespace-only trim on commit = cancel (matches the sidebar/dialog trim guard); an unchanged name is also a no-op. Commit calls the shared `useWindowRename()` hook (¬ß Shared window rename below) ‚Äî optimistic store rename + toast on error ‚Äî then optimistically sets the display; the name-change effect replays the sweep when the store-driven `name` prop settles.

**Keyboard path (Constitution V)**: the command-palette `Window: Rename` action dispatches a `window-heading:rename` `CustomEvent` (mirroring `theme-selector:open`); a document-level listener in `WindowHeading` enters inline edit. The former rename **modal dialog was retired** ‚Äî the palette was its sole entry point; see ¬ß Keyboard Shortcuts (the palette rename action) and ¬ß Component Conventions (the shared `Dialog`). The `use-dialog-state.ts` window-rename state (`openRenameDialog`/`handleRename`/`executeRenameWindow` + `lastRenameWindowRef` + the `renameWindow` import) was deleted along with the `<Dialog title="Rename window">` JSX in `app.tsx`; only the SESSION rename dialog remains there.

**External-switch cancel**: a `prevIdentityRef` effect keyed on `${server}:${windowId}` cancels an in-progress edit when the window identity changes out from under it (another client / tmux switching the route) ‚Äî committing the typed name onto the newly-navigated window would rename the wrong window.

### Display-only page headings (`PageHeadingDisplay` in `top-bar.tsx`, `260704-pr0p`)

The board/server/host siblings of `WindowHeading` ‚Äî a `PageHeadingDisplay({ prefix, name, solo?, ariaLabel })` that renders the same `PageType: name` two-tone identity via the SAME `useBootSweep`/`SweepCells` primitive, but with NO rename affordance (boards/servers have no rename API; the host mode has no instance). The static prefix span is `hidden sm:inline` (same mobile rule as terminal); the `solo` variant (host) renders the single word primary-medium and visible at all breakpoints. Hover replays the sweep behind the 140ms intent; mount + displayed-name-change replay via the same `null`-seeded `prevNameRef` effect; reduced motion skips. **A11y**: the identity carries a STABLE `aria-label` (the churn glyphs are `aria-hidden` inside `SweepCells`) placed on a `role="group"` wrapper ‚Äî `aria-label` is prohibited on the implicit `role="generic"` of a bare `<div>`/`<span>`, so `role="group"` is what makes it a valid, screen-reader-stable accessible name (`260704-pr0p` rework N3). No `<h1>` is added to the top bar.

**Tests**: `top-bar.test.tsx` covers the heading display/edit states (click ‚Üí input, Enter commits via `renameWindow`, Escape/empty-trim cancel), the `window-heading:rename` CustomEvent entering edit, AND per-mode heading coverage (terminal `Window:` prefix sibling ‚Äî `Window:` since `260714-uco1`, board `Board:` + board switcher in the center, server `tmux Server:`, solo `Host`; board left nav shows only counts/hint ‚Äî no `Board ‚ñ∏`, no left board name; server left nav has no `aria-current` leaf). E2e `tests/e2e/window-heading.spec.ts` (+ sibling `.spec.md`, per the constitution's Test Companion Docs rule) covers, documented 1:1 in the `.spec.md`: the terminal heading renders the name once with a static `Window:` prefix sibling (NOT a trailing breadcrumb crumb); click ‚Üí inline input ‚Üí Enter commits (sidebar + heading reflect the new name); Escape cancels (window id unchanged); the palette `window-heading:rename` CustomEvent enters inline edit; the 375px bar stays single-line with no horizontal overflow; hover-treatment classes present and unchanged under `reducedMotion: "reduce"`; the board/server/host centered headings render with their prefixes; the `[ SESSIONS‚ñä ]` section-heading shape; a motion-opted-in **boot-sweep** e2e (hover the heading ‚Üí an `.rk-typed-cursor` cell attaches ‚Üí resolves to rest ‚Äî `260704-pr0p` SHOULD-FIX 2, since the units stub `matchMedia` to reduced-motion and never exercise the sweep behaviorally); and a reduced-context check that the sweep never starts (JS-gated).

### Shared window rename (`useWindowRename`, `hooks/use-window-rename.ts`, `260703-5ilm`)

`useWindowRename()` returns `execute(server, session, windowId, newName)` ‚Äî the ONE optimistic window-rename action, used by BOTH the top-bar `WindowHeading` AND the sidebar inline rename (`sidebar/index.tsx:398`), so the two surfaces rename identically. It stamps the window store's `pendingName` (`renameWindow`) on `onOptimistic`, rolls back via `clearRename` on failure with a toast, and clears the pending marker on settle (SSE snapshot then becomes authoritative). The captured `(server, session, windowId)` is held in a `lastRenameRef` so rollback/settle target the right entry even if the caller re-renders between execute and resolution. Callers own their own trim/empty-name guards before calling (rename is unconditional inside the hook). This extraction replaced the sidebar's former inline ~25-line `executeRenameWindow` `useOptimisticAction` block (deleted by `260703-5ilm`). Session rename is NOT part of this hook ‚Äî it keeps its own dialog/inline path (¬ß Sidebar ‚Üí Session rename).

### Hover-Animation Vocabulary (`260703-5ilm`)

A site-wide motion map where each treatment encodes **exactly one** category of element, so motion carries meaning instead of noise. The shared color cue: **the animated element turns `--color-accent-green` while it animates** (the brand chip on glitch-hover, the boot-sweep cursor + name-churn cells, both caret variants, the stepping brackets ‚Äî user-requested ‚Äî including the glint: the sweep strip is accent-green-tinted and the hovered chip's border + glyph flip green for the hover duration, the "green line"). **Scope note** (`260704-pr0p`): the boot-sweep green is now PER-CELL ‚Äî only the single cursor cell and the unresolved name-churn glyphs are green; the heading container does NOT tint green wholesale (the earlier decode did), so resolved cells settle to their own rest color and the two-tone reveal reads left-to-right. All utilities live in `globals.css` (beside the `logo-chase` keyframes / `coarse` variant; Tailwind CSS 4). Under `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` the contract is **animations zeroed, not styling removed**: the CSS gate zeroes every keyframe animation (classes stay in the DOM ‚Äî that is the test seam), the JS treatments (decode, typed sweep) skip themselves by reading the same media query, and static hover styling (e.g. the glint's green border/glyph flip) remains ‚Äî a color change is not motion. No pixel assertions in tests ‚Äî treatments are asserted via class-presence + reduced-motion emulation, plus one behavioral guard for the caret (below).

| Category | Treatment | Mechanism |
|----------|-----------|-----------|
| **Brand** | glitch | `.rk-brand-glitch` on the top-left "Run Kit" brand anchor ‚Äî one-shot `@keyframes rk-glitch` RGB-split `text-shadow` (~300ms, `steps(2)`, ¬±2px split) on `:hover`, plus `color: var(--color-accent-green)` for the hover duration (the color snap is what makes the glitch read at 11.5px; the split is texture ‚Äî the shadow alone was barely visible). Wordmark hidden below `sm`, so on mobile only the icon jitters (accepted). |
| **Top-bar page heading** | boot sweep | JS in `top-bar.tsx` ‚Äî the shared `useBootSweep` hook + `SweepCells` renderer (see ¬ß Window Heading / ¬ß Display-only page headings), NOT a CSS class. ONE inverse-video accent-green cursor at `DECODE_FRAME_MS` (28ms/cell) sweeps `PageType:` + space + `name`: over the PREFIX it types like TypedLabel (`rk-typed-off` ahead / `rk-typed-cursor` cursor cell / `text-secondary` resolved); over the NAME the cells right of the cursor churn `DECODE_GLYPHS` in accent-green from frame 0, each locked to its true char as the cursor arrives, resolved cells settling to semibold `text-primary` (spaces preserved). Reuses the `rk-typed-*` cell classes + `DECODE_*` constants ‚Äî no class of its own. Replaced `260703-5ilm`'s terminal-only "decode" scramble (which flipped the whole heading green). |
| **Section headings** | brackets + caret | `.rk-bracket-group` scoped to `SectionHeading`'s inner bracket cluster ONLY (not the row/rule/`side`). On group `:hover` the `.rk-bracket-open`/`.rk-bracket-close` spans step outward `translateX(‚àì3px)` + turn `--color-accent-green` (transform only ‚Äî no layout shift), and a `.rk-bracket-caret` (always-reserved `1ch` cell, accent-green, transparent at rest so the closing bracket never shifts) blinks `‚ñä` (`@keyframes rk-caret-blink`, 1.06s `steps(1)`). Moved from the retired `PageHeading` to the in-page section labels by `260704-pr0p`. See ¬ß Section Heading. |
| **Section labels** | typed sweep | `TypedLabel` (`components/typed-label.tsx`) ‚Äî on hover the label fades (`.rk-typed-off`, 26% opacity) and an inverse-video cursor (`.rk-typed-cursor`, accent-green cell OVER the character ‚Äî a terminal block cursor sitting on text) sweeps from the FIRST cell, "typing" each character back to full brightness (`.rk-typed-on`); after the pass the label holds bright (`rk-typed-done`) until pointer-leave. Fixed ~350ms TOTAL pass regardless of length (per-cell = 350/len clamped 20‚Äì60ms) so all labels read as one gesture; width never changes (the cursor occupies its cell). JS-driven (the frame states are the `globals.css` `.rk-typed-*` classes); reduced motion skips the sweep entirely in JS. Applied to the sidebar panel titles (`collapsible-panel.tsx`) and the sidebar `Sessions` region heading (`sidebar/index.tsx`) directly, and ‚Äî since `260704-pr0p` wrapped them in `SectionHeading` ‚Äî INSIDE the brackets on the tmux Server page's `Sessions` heading (`session-tiles.tsx`) and the four Host-page zone `h2`s (Host Health / Boards / Tmux Servers / Services, `host-overview-page.tsx`), where the typed sweep and the brackets+caret hover compose on one element. The sidebar labels are deliberately NOT bracket targets (typed-sweep only). Decorative ‚Äî headings stay non-interactive-looking at rest. |
| **Buttons** | CRT glint + green line | `.rk-glint` ‚Äî `position:relative; overflow:hidden` + an `::after` skewed accent-green highlight strip sweeping across the button face on `:hover` (`@keyframes rk-glint-sweep`, ~450ms one-shot), plus `.rk-glint:hover:not(:disabled)` flipping border + glyph to `--color-accent-green` (unlayered rule, so it beats the chips' Tailwind hover utilities without touching call sites; chosen over a fill/inverse cell so hover never reads as the armed state's solid accent fill). Applied to every top-bar right-cluster chip (SplitButton, ClosePaneButton, TerminalFontControl, NotificationControl, ThemeToggle, FixedWidthToggle, BoardAutofitToggle, HelpLink) AND the bottom-bar `KBD_CLASS` buttons. `overflow:hidden` is verified safe ‚Äî the font/bell popovers are SIBLINGS of their trigger buttons, not children, so clipping never clips a popover. |

**Typed-sweep history note**: the section-label treatment was originally a CSS-only hover caret (`.rk-label-caret::after`), replaced wholesale by the `TypedLabel` typed sweep after a design iteration (user picked the inverse-video-cursor variation from the heading-lab demo). The old CSS classes are deleted; the e2e guard now asserts the sweep behaviorally (cursor cell attaches ‚Üí `rk-typed-done` lands ‚Üí unhover resets). The `.rk-bracket-caret` is unrelated and unchanged ‚Äî a reserved `1ch` blinking caret cell inside the bracket group, now carried by `SectionHeading` (was `PageHeading`, `260704-pr0p`). Note the section labels now compose BOTH vocabularies on one element: the typed sweep (TypedLabel, inside the brackets) AND the brackets+caret hover (the `rk-bracket-group` cluster around them).

### Theme System

> Full spec: [`docs/specs/themes.md`](../../specs/themes.md) ‚Äî architecture, ANSI palette structure, tmux colour mapping, import script usage, persistence model.

Palette-based theme model: each theme defines a `ThemePalette` with 22 canonical terminal colors ‚Äî `foreground`, `background`, `cursorColor`, `cursorText`, `selectionBackground`, `selectionForeground`, plus 16 ANSI colors (indices 0-15) as a fixed-length readonly tuple. The `Theme` type has shape `{ id, name, category, palette }` ‚Äî no `colors` or `themeColor` properties (both replaced by derivation from palette).

20 built-in themes (14 dark + 6 light) defined in `app/frontend/src/themes.ts` with canonical ANSI palettes sourced from iTerm2-Color-Schemes / official theme repos. Three consumers derive from the same palette:

1. **Web UI CSS** ‚Äî `deriveUIColors(palette, category)` produces 8 `UIColors` keys (`bgPrimary`, `bgCard`, `bgInset`, `textPrimary`, `textSecondary`, `border`, `accent`, `accentGreen`). Derivation: `bgPrimary` = background, `bgCard` = lighten/darken background, `bgInset` = darken background, `textPrimary` = foreground, `textSecondary` = ansi[8] (bright black), `border` = blend(fg, bg, 0.25), `accent` = ansi[4] (blue), `accentGreen` = ansi[2] (green). Color utility helpers (`hexToRgb`, `rgbToHex`, `lightenHex`, `darkenHex`, `blendHex`) are module-private. CSS custom properties (`--color-bg-primary`, etc.) applied via inline styles on `document.documentElement.style` overriding `globals.css` fallbacks.
2. **xterm.js canvas** ‚Äî `deriveXtermTheme(palette)` produces an xterm.js `ITheme` with all 22 colors mapped (background, foreground, cursor, cursorAccent, selectionBackground, selectionForeground, and 16 named ANSI colors black through brightWhite). Terminal content (syntax highlighting, colored prompts, git diff output) matches the selected theme.
3. **tmux chrome** ‚Äî `configs/tmux/default.conf` uses ANSI `colour{N}` indices (colour0-colour15) instead of hardcoded hex. Because tmux renders its chrome as escape sequences that xterm.js interprets, changing the xterm.js ANSI palette automatically themes tmux status bar, pane borders, and pane-border-format. No runtime `tmux set -g` calls needed ‚Äî the tmux.conf is static.

`data-theme` attribute set to theme's `category` ("dark" or "light") for CSS branching. Theme preferences persisted to both backend API (`GET/PUT /api/settings/theme` writing `~/.rk/settings.yaml`) and localStorage as synchronous cache. Three settings: `theme` (mode: `"system"` or specific ID), `theme_dark` (preferred dark theme, default `"default-dark"`), `theme_light` (preferred light theme, default `"default-light"`). localStorage keys: `runkit-theme`, `runkit-theme-dark`, `runkit-theme-light`. On init, API is canonical source; localStorage is the fast fallback if API fails. Unrecognized `theme` values fall back to `"system"`, while unrecognized `theme_dark`/`theme_light` values fall back to `"default-dark"`/`"default-light"`. PUT accepts partial updates (load-then-merge).

**ThemeToggle** (top bar): Normal click cycles `system ‚Üí default-light ‚Üí default-dark`. **Ctrl+Click / Cmd+Click** dispatches `"theme-selector:open"` CustomEvent to open the theme selector.

**Theme Selector** (`app/frontend/src/components/theme-selector.tsx`): Modal overlay matching CommandPalette structure (fixed z-50, backdrop, max-w-lg at 20vh). Search input filters by name (case-insensitive). Themes grouped under "Dark" / "Light" category headers. Arrow key navigation wraps and skips headers. Mouse hover and arrow navigation trigger live preview via `previewTheme()` ‚Äî CSS custom properties update in real-time. Enter confirms (persists to API + localStorage), Escape/outside-click reverts to original theme via `cancelPreview()`. Opens via `"theme-selector:open"` custom event (same pattern as `"palette:open"`). Theme rows display multi-color palette swatches showing background plus representative ANSI colors (red, green, yellow, blue, magenta, cyan) instead of a single-color swatch.

**Command palette**: "Theme: Select Theme" action dispatches `"theme-selector:open"`. Individual "Theme: System", "Theme: Light", "Theme: Dark" quick-switch actions retained.

**ThemeProvider** (`app/frontend/src/contexts/theme-context.tsx`): `useTheme()` returns `{ preference, resolved, theme, themeDark, themeLight }`. `useThemeActions()` returns `{ setTheme, previewTheme, cancelPreview }`. Preview applies colors to DOM without persistence. Cancel reverts to the last persisted theme. Uses stable `actionsRef` pattern for callback identity. On init: calls `getThemePreference()` from API (returns `{ theme, themeDark, themeLight }`), falls back to localStorage / defaults if API fails. Per-mode theme resolution: in `"system"` mode, resolves to the user's preferred dark or light theme based on OS `prefers-color-scheme`, falling back to `DEFAULT_DARK_THEME` / `DEFAULT_LIGHT_THEME` if the stored ID is invalid. `setTheme` with a specific theme ID saves it to the matching per-mode slot (by `category`), keeps preference as `"system"` (preserving OS auto-toggle), and persists all three values to API and localStorage. `setTheme("system")` resets to system mode without changing per-mode prefs. Backend is canonical source of truth; localStorage is the fast fallback.

### Breadcrumb Dropdowns

Session and window name text are the dropdown triggers. Clicking/tapping the name opens the respective dropdown. No split click-target pattern ‚Äî the name itself is the trigger. The session name shown in the breadcrumb is the **snapshot-derived** owning session of the active `@N` (since `260529-jad6` dropped `$session` from the URL), not a URL segment.

**Session dropdown**: Lists all tmux sessions. Current session highlighted with `text-accent`. Selecting navigates to the session's first window by its window ID (`/{server}/{windows[0].windowId}` ‚Äî 2-segment since `260529-jad6`). First item: `+ New Session` action ‚Äî triggers instant session creation (no dialog).

**Window switcher** (relocated out of the breadcrumb by `260703-5ilm`): Lists all windows in the current session. Current window highlighted (`w.windowId === currentWindow.windowId`). Selecting navigates to `/{server}/{windowId}` (2-segment since `260529-jad6`). First item: `+ New Window` action (creates new window in current session). **No longer a trailing breadcrumb crumb** ‚Äî it now renders as a **label-less bare-`‚ñæ` `BreadcrumbDropdown`** in the top bar's center cell, beside the centered `WindowHeading` (name-click = edit, `‚ñæ`-click = switch); the window name lives once in the heading. Still carries `title="Window"` and stays visible on mobile (the only in-bar window switcher once the crumb moved). See ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell / ¬ß Window Heading.

**Board switcher** (`BoardSwitcher` in `top-bar.tsx`, relocated to the center cell by `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep`): the board mode's `‚ñæ` dropdown ‚Äî lists the cross-server boards + a `‚Üê Sessions` navigate action. Moved from the left `BoardModeBreadcrumb` (the old `Board ‚ñ∏ {name} ‚ñæ` cluster) to sit beside the centered `Board: <board>` display heading, mirroring the window switcher's center-cell placement. The board name is display-only (no rename API); the `‚ñæ` is the sole board affordance in the bar. The left nav keeps only the pane/server counts + `‚åò[‚åò] cycle` hint (`BoardModeInfo`). See ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell / Board.

**Action items in dropdowns**: `BreadcrumbDropdown` accepts an optional `action` prop of type `{ label: string; onAction: () => void }`. When provided, the action item renders before the selection list, separated by a divider (`border-t border-border`). Action items use `text-text-primary` styling (not `text-accent`), close the dropdown on click, and are excluded from ArrowUp/ArrowDown keyboard navigation among selection items.

**Optional `secondaryAction`** (since `260713-sbk1-web-spawn-agent`): a second leading action of the same `{ label, onAction }` shape, rendered below `action` and above the divider ‚Äî **only honored when `action` is also present**. Its sole call site is the terminal-mode window-switcher dropdown, which renders `+ New Window` (`action`) and `+ New Agent` (`secondaryAction`) as two stacked leading buttons. The two actions occupy dropdown indices `0..offset-1` (leading actions) with selection items following at `offset..N-1`; the internal `actionRef` singleton became an `actionRefs` array and the focus-index `offset` is now the count of present leading actions ‚Äî so the keyboard-nav index math generalizes to N leading actions while every **other** call site (session switcher, board switcher) that passes only `action` keeps its single-action behavior byte-for-byte. This minimal second-prop shape was chosen over a generic `actions: []` array (only one call site needs two actions, and an array would churn every call site plus the focus-index logic). See ¬ß Spawn-Agent Dialog.

**Dropdown component** (`app/frontend/src/components/breadcrumb-dropdown.tsx`): Reusable dropdown with outside-click dismiss, Escape dismiss, ArrowUp/ArrowDown keyboard navigation, ARIA `role="menu"`/`role="menuitem"`. Styled with `bg-bg-primary border-border shadow-2xl`, matching bottom-bar Fn key dropdown pattern. Name text serves as the trigger (44px on touch devices via `coarse:min-h-[44px]`), wrapped in a `min-w-0 truncate` span. When the trigger has a label (`icon` prop set) it renders a **persistent `‚ñæ` caret** after the label (`aria-hidden`, `ml-1 shrink-0 text-base` ‚Äî 16px, user-tuned for visibility) ‚Äî the always-visible "opens a menu" affordance distinguishing dropdown crumbs from link crumbs (`260702-6m46`; see ¬ß Crumb Affordance Vocabulary). A label-less trigger already IS a bare caret (`‚ñæ` fallback) and gets no second one. Long names truncated via `max-w-[240px]`.

Connection indicator: green/gray dot only (no text label), driven by `isConnected` from ChromeProvider (set by each page from `useSessions`).

**Open menu escapes any `overflow:hidden` ancestor via `position: fixed` (`260715-q8ey-top-bar-overlap-fixes`).** The open `role="menu"` element renders **`position: fixed` anchored to the trigger's viewport rect** ‚Äî it measures `buttonRef.getBoundingClientRect()` on open and positions its top-left at `rect.bottom + gap` / `rect.left`, recomputing (or closing) on `scroll`/`resize` (capture-phase, so a scrolling ancestor container is heard) so it never detaches from the moving trigger. It was previously `absolute top-full` inside its own `relative` wrapper. **The reusable invariant ‚Äî clip-backstop vs. contained popover**: when you add `overflow-hidden` (or `overflow-clip`) to a container that also *holds* a popover, a plain `absolute` popover inside it gets **both clipped AND focus-scroll-displaced** ‚Äî `overflow:hidden` turns the container into a scroll box, and the menu's focus-on-open `scrollIntoView` then scrolls the whole container's content out of its own clip box. This is exactly the bug the `q8ey` nav clip-backstop (¬ß Center-heading ‚Ä¶ ‚Üí degradation ladder step 3) introduced on the session-switcher menu (empirically: post-clip the menu landed off-viewport at y‚âà-75 with an empty hit-test; pre-clip it rendered visible at y‚âà37). The nav clip is a user-approved requirement, so the resolution is to let the menu **escape the clip context**, not weaken the clip ‚Äî and `position: fixed` is viewport-relative, so no `overflow:hidden` ancestor can clip it. `overflow-clip` on the container would have fixed only the focus-scroll (a clip box is not a scroll container), not the clipping itself. Because the escape lives in the shared `BreadcrumbDropdown` component, it applies identically to **all four call sites** (session crumb, hierarchy ‚ñæ, window switcher, board switcher); it keeps `z-50`, the `min-w-[160px] max-w-[240px]` sizing, and the existing click-outside / Escape / Arrow-key focus behavior. **Rule for future clips**: adding `overflow-hidden` to any container that contains a popover requires that popover to escape via fixed/portal positioning, or the popover breaks.

### Crumb Affordance Vocabulary (`260702-6m46`)

Breadcrumb crumbs advertise their interactivity WITHOUT hover ‚Äî a two-affordance vocabulary where the crumbs that remain are all interactive (since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` moved every current-page LEAF out of the left nav into the centered heading, ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar), the "you are here" signal is the centered heading itself, not a no-affordance crumb). The cases:

- **Link crumbs** (brand, server link) ‚Äî carry the shared `LINK_CRUMB_CLASS` constant (`top-bar.tsx`): a **bordered chip** (`rounded border border-border hover:border-text-secondary px-1.5 py-0.5 text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary transition-colors`), reusing the right cluster's "bordered = clickable" language. The user compared three candidates live (chip / accent color / dotted underline) and picked the chip; the unused variant definitions were removed at lock-in. *(Accent color was rejected ‚Äî hue is reserved by the StatusDot phases; dotted underline was rejected ‚Äî it left the mobile icon-only brand with no affordance, and text-decoration doesn't propagate into an anchor's flex children, so the wordmark needed a `[text-decoration:inherit]` patch that the chip doesn't.)*
- **Dropdown triggers** (session ‚Äî and the relocated window/board switchers) ‚Äî carry the persistent `‚ñæ` caret inside `BreadcrumbDropdown` (see ¬ß Breadcrumb Dropdowns). Signals "opens a switcher", distinct from "navigates". Note the **window switcher** (since `260703-5ilm`) AND the **board switcher** (since `260704-pr0p`) are no longer in the left breadcrumb ‚Äî both are bare-`‚ñæ` `BreadcrumbDropdown`s in the top bar's center cell beside their headings (¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) center cell), using the same caret affordance.
- **Current-page leaf** ‚Äî since `260704-pr0p` there is NO leaf crumb in the left nav; the current page's identity is the **centered `PageType: name` heading**. The former `aria-current="page"` server-name leaf on the tmux Server page moved to the center as `tmux Server: <server>`. (The historical "the absence of an affordance marks the leaf" case no longer applies to a crumb ‚Äî the heading carries the "you are here" role.)

*Why not hover-only cues*: the pre-`260702-6m46` `hover:text-text-primary` cue was invisible to first-time users and absent entirely on touch.

### Section Heading (`section-heading.tsx`, `260704-pr0p`; retired `page-heading.tsx`)

A shared `SectionHeading({ label, side?, className? })` renders a one-line **bracketed BBS-menu-tag** SECTION heading ‚Äî `[ SESSIONS‚ñä ]‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ side`. It is the successor to the retired `PageHeading` (`page-heading.tsx` + `page-heading.test.tsx` DELETED by `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep`): the bracket idiom that used to name the PAGE in the page body now names in-page SECTIONS, because page identity moved to the top-bar center heading (¬ß Chrome (Top Bar), ¬ß Canonical page names ‚Äî Vocabulary Split). This is the intake's "move, don't copy" applied to the bracket vocabulary ‚Äî the brackets stayed on screen but shifted from page-level to section-level.

- **Structure**: an outer `<div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">` (a div, NOT a span ‚Äî it contains an `<h2>`, and a span may not contain flow content). The inner `rk-bracket-group flex items-center gap-1.5 min-w-0 shrink-0 max-w-[60%]` cluster holds: the `[` open bracket, an `<h2 className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wide text-text-secondary">` wrapping `<TypedLabel text={label} />` (so the section-label typed-sweep lives INSIDE the brackets ‚Äî ¬ß Hover-Animation Vocabulary), the always-reserved `‚ñä` caret cell, then the `]` close bracket. A `flex-1 min-w-4 border-t border-border` fills the middle as the rule (a CSS border ‚Äî responsive, no literal `‚îÄ` glyphs to overflow at 375px); an optional right-aligned `side` slot (`text-sm text-text-secondary truncate shrink-0`) sits after the rule when provided.
- **Accessibility**: the `[`/`]` brackets, the `‚ñä` caret cell, and the rule are `aria-hidden`; the `<h2>` is the accessible structure and its accessible name is the label text ONLY (uppercase styling matches the former bare `<h2>` idiom). No `<h1>` anywhere (the top bar adds none either ‚Äî ¬ß Display-only page headings).
- **Bracket hover treatment** (brackets+caret = section-heading vocabulary, moved from PageHeading by `260704-pr0p`): the inner bracket cluster carries `rk-bracket-group`, scoping the hover treatment to THIS cluster ONLY ‚Äî the rule and `side` slot are outside it and never trigger it. On group hover the `[`/`]` spans (`.rk-bracket .rk-bracket-open`/`.rk-bracket-close`) step outward `translateX(‚àì3px)` + turn accent (transform only, no layout shift), and the **always-reserved `.rk-bracket-caret` cell** (fixed `1ch`, transparent at rest, sitting AFTER the label and BEFORE the closing bracket ‚Üí `[ SESSIONS‚ñä ]`) blinks its `‚ñä`. All disabled under `prefers-reduced-motion`. See ¬ß Hover-Animation Vocabulary. (This reserved-caret is NOT the section-label typed sweep, which lives in the `TypedLabel` inside the brackets ‚Äî the two vocabularies compose on this one element.)
- **tmux Server page** (`/$server`): since `260715-zs1y` a page-level `<SectionHeading label="tmux Server Overview" />` heads the scroll area (¬ß Page Overview Headings), then `<SectionHeading label="Sessions" side={"{N} sessions, {M} windows"} />` precedes the session-tile grid (`session-tiles.tsx`). The server-view stats ‚Äî formerly the plain stats line, then the PageHeading `side` ‚Äî ride the `Sessions` heading's `side` slot, right-aligned after the rule.
- **Host-page zones** (`/`): since `260715-zs1y` a page-level `<SectionHeading label="Host Overview" />` heads the scroll container (¬ß Page Overview Headings), above the four zone `<h2>`s ‚Äî `Host Health` / `Boards` / `Tmux Servers` / `Services` ‚Äî which became `<SectionHeading label=... className="mb-2" />` (`host-overview-page.tsx`), replacing the former bare `<h2><TypedLabel/></h2>` and the removed `[ cockpit ]` PageHeading row (the `[ cockpit ]` label predates the `260715-zs1y` rename). The zone headings' `side` slots stay **empty** (reserved for the server-view stats relocation, plan assumption #4); each zone's existing inline metadata (live hostname / `{N} boards` / `{N} servers`) stays in the zone BODY at its original `text-xs` sizing right below the heading ‚Äî NOT relocated to `side` ("no side text" meant no relocated stats, not deletion of existing metadata; `260704-pr0p` SHOULD-FIX 1 restored this after an initial version wrongly parked it in `side`).
- **Tests**: `section-heading.test.tsx` asserts the `<h2>` accessible name equals the label (brackets/caret/rule `aria-hidden`), the optional `side` slot renders after the rule, and the `TypedLabel` is present inside the brackets. `host-overview-page.test.tsx` (renamed from `server-list-page.test.tsx` in `260715-zs1y`) asserts no level-1 heading remains (PageHeading `[ cockpit ]` `<h1>` gone) and the four zone `<h2>` labels still render in order (Host Health ‚Üí Boards ‚Üí Tmux Servers ‚Üí Services), plus (since `260715-zs1y`) that the `Host Overview` page heading renders. `host-overview-page.test.tsx`'s previous `PageHeading` coupling was removed.

### Page Overview Headings (`260715-zs1y-host-tmux-server-rename`)

The `260715-zs1y` vocabulary rename (Cockpit ‚Üí Host, Server Cabin ‚Üí tmux Server; ¬ß Canonical page names) added **two new in-page `SectionHeading` headings** ‚Äî the only behavior change in that otherwise copy/identifier-only change. Each is a page-level heading at the TOP of its page's scroll container, above the page's first zone/section, reusing the existing `SectionHeading` component (¬ß Section Heading) ‚Äî no new heading style was invented, and both inherit `SectionHeading`/`TypedLabel` `prefers-reduced-motion` behavior (static under reduced motion):

- **"Host Overview"** ‚Äî on `/` (`host-overview-page.tsx`), the first child inside the `overflow-y-auto` scroll container, ABOVE the HOST HEALTH zone (so the page reads `[ HOST OVERVIEW ]` then the four zones). Distinct from the top-bar center-cell solo `Host` identity heading ‚Äî this is the in-page overview label, that is the chrome page-type identity.
- **"tmux Server Overview"** ‚Äî on `/$server` (`session-tiles.tsx`, the no-window `SessionTiles` view), the first child of the scroll area, ABOVE the existing `[ SESSIONS ]` `SectionHeading`. It renders **only** in the no-window `/$server` view; navigating into a window (`/$server/$window`) does not mount `SessionTiles`, so the heading is absent there. Distinct from the top-bar `tmux Server: <server>` center-cell identity heading.

Coverage: `host-overview-page.test.tsx` asserts the "Host Overview" heading renders; `tests/e2e/window-heading.spec.ts` (+ `.spec.md`) asserts both "Host Overview" (`/`) and "tmux Server Overview" (`/$server`) in-page headings.

**FixedWidthToggle** (in the top-bar right cluster): part of the route-agnostic FixedWidth ‚Üí Notification ‚Üí Theme block (before the right-most connection dot; see ¬ß Chrome (Top Bar) for the full cluster order). Self-contained component using `useChrome()`/`useChromeDispatch()`. Route-agnostic ‚Äî renders in every mode including host (`260509-17m3-rotated-shell-layout` lifted it out of the `currentWindow &&` block ‚Äî fixed-width is a viewport preference, not a per-window setting; it stays even on the server-less Host page since fixed-width constrains any surface). Touch target: `coarse:min-h-[30px] coarse:min-w-[30px]`. Since `260715-h1ck` it is the L1 registry `fixed-width` candidate (gated `modes: ["terminal"]`, `hidden: !currentWindow` per the pyramid table above ‚Äî the "route-agnostic, renders in every mode" wording predates the `260704-9o7k` L1 demotion and the pyramid table is authoritative): no longer `hidden sm:flex`-wrapped, its menu row is a "Fixed width" `role="menuitemcheckbox"` and it is reachable below `sm` instead of vanishing.

**TerminalFontControl** (`top-bar.tsx`, placed near `FixedWidthToggle`; `260613-oo89-terminal-font-size-control`): a compact combo `[‚àí] {size} [+]` + reset for the global terminal font preference (see ¬ß Terminal Font Size). Self-contained sub-component (mirrors the `FixedWidthToggle` function-component shape) reading `useChromeState()`/`useChromeDispatch()` and `TERMINAL_FONT_BOUNDS`. The ‚àí button is disabled at `min` (8), the + button at `max` (24); the value label shows the effective size; reset calls `resetTerminalFont`. aria-labels `Decrease terminal font` / `Increase terminal font` / `Reset terminal font`; established top-bar `coarse:36px`-square touch sizing.

### Sidebar Kill Controls

- **Session row ‚úï**: Always-visible ‚úï button on session rows with red hover. Normal click opens confirmation dialog: "Kill session **{name}** and all {N} windows?" **Ctrl+Click / Cmd+Click** bypasses the confirmation dialog and kills immediately (best-effort `.catch(() => {})`).
- **Window row ‚úï**: Hover-reveal ‚úï button on window rows (always visible on touch devices via `coarse:opacity-100`). Normal click opens confirmation dialog: "Kill window in **{session}**?" **Ctrl+Click / Cmd+Click** bypasses the confirmation dialog and kills immediately (best-effort `.catch(() => {})`).

The Ctrl+Click force-kill pattern matches the established "modifier = power action" convention: ThemeToggle uses Ctrl+Click to open the theme selector instead of cycling. Modifier detection uses `e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey` (Ctrl on Linux/Windows, Cmd on macOS).

## Sidebar

`app/frontend/src/components/sidebar/` ‚Äî session/window tree navigation. The sidebar is decomposed into an orchestrator and seven sub-components:

- `index.tsx` ‚Äî `Sidebar` orchestrator; owns all state (`collapsed`, `killTarget`, `editingWindow`, `editingSession`, `dragSource`, `dropTarget`, `sessionDropTarget`) and all `useOptimisticAction` hooks. Accepts `metrics` and `isConnected` props for HostPanel
- `session-row.tsx` ‚Äî `SessionRow` (exported as `memo(SessionRowInner)`); renders the session header row (chevron, name) plus a **trailing hover-revealed icon cluster** in fixed order `[üé® palette/color] [ü§ñ bot spawn] [+ create window] [‚úï kill]` ‚Äî the bot button (`gsmu`) sits immediately **LEFT of `+`** so `+`/`‚úï` keep their muscle-memory edge positions; handles cross-session drag-over styling; all event handlers passed as props (stable identity-arg `useCallback`s ‚Äî see ¬ß Render Performance). **Session-row icon cluster** (the spawn-agent trigger): each icon button shares the same affordance classes as its palette sibling (`text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 coarse:opacity-100`, `min-h-[24px] coarse:min-h-[36px]`). The **bot button** (`onSpawnAgent && (‚Ä¶)`) renders **only when an `onSpawnAgent?: (server, session) => void` handler is present** (mirroring the optional `onColorChange` pattern), carries `aria-label={`Spawn agent in ${session.name}`}`, and on click does `e.stopPropagation()` then `onSpawnAgent(server, name)` ‚Äî passing the ROW's explicit `{server, session}` (the spawn target). Its glyph is `BotIcon` from `sidebar/icons.tsx` ‚Äî a lucide-style `bot` (robot head: antenna + rounded head with two eye dots + side ports) stroke SVG matching the `PaletteIcon` idiom (`stroke="currentColor"`, `strokeWidth={2}`, `aria-hidden`, 24-unit viewBox + 13px default size). **Prop threading** (`gsmu`): `onSpawnAgent` is optional on `SidebarProps` ‚Üí threaded through `ServerGroupProps`/`ServerGroupInner` ‚Üí `SessionRow` (mirroring `onColorChange`); the board-route sidebar passes NO handler, so the bot button is hidden there (Non-Goal ‚Äî later wiring is cheap via the optional prop). See ¬ß Spawn-Agent Dialog for the dialog it opens.
- `window-row.tsx` ‚Äî `WindowRow` (exported as `memo(WindowRowInner)`); renders a single window row (a leading unified `<StatusDot>` + name) plus the absolutely-positioned hover-icon cluster (pin / color swatch / kill); handles drag-and-drop and inline rename display; all event handlers passed as props. **Row Minimalism** (`260706-y1ar`): the trailing status cluster ‚Äî the fab stage word AND the `WindowDuration`/`TickingDuration` duration leaves (and their per-second `useNow()` tick) ‚Äî were **removed**; the leading `<StatusDot>` is the row's ONLY status signal, so the component is again purely presentational except for its hover-icon state (¬ß Window rows / Row Minimalism). The icon cluster is inert at rest (`pointer-events-none` + hover/coarse/focus restore). Does NOT render any full PR line (the `PrStatusLine` component it never rendered was removed entirely by `260715-jykd`) ‚Äî its single leading dot carries all status: since `260706-y1ar` the dot is the palette-v3 two-family ladder + additive waiting halo (¬ß Status Dot).
- `collapsible-panel.tsx` ‚Äî `CollapsiblePanel`; reusable collapsible container with header (title + chevron) and localStorage open/closed state persistence via `storageKey` prop. Two modes: (a) legacy `max-height` CSS transition when `resizable` is absent/false (preserves existing Window/Host panel behaviour); (b) resizable mode (opt-in via `resizable` prop) ‚Äî renders a 6px `ns-resize` drag handle at the bottom, persists user-set height to `localStorage[${storageKey}-height]`, and supports `defaultHeight`/`minHeight`/`maxHeight` props. `maxHeight` accepts a number or a `calc(100vh - Npx)` string form (parsed at drag time using `window.innerHeight`). Mobile breakpoint (`@media (pointer: coarse), (max-width: 639px)`) hides the drag handle and pins the content area to the `mobileHeight` prop (default 56px). All localStorage access wrapped in try/catch. **Header tint**: `tint` prop (`RowTint | null`) paints the header background. By default (legacy mode) the header uses `tint.base` with a `tint.base` ‚Üî `tint.hover` swap on hover. When `tintOnlyWhenCollapsed` is set, the tint is applied only while the panel is collapsed ‚Äî and the shade switches to `tint.selected` with the hover swap disabled (stays flat), because in that mode the header is standing in for the selected item inside and a less-saturated hover would read as an inverted effect. `ServerPanel` is the only current consumer of `tintOnlyWhenCollapsed`; the legacy `base`/`hover` behavior is preserved for forward compatibility
- `status-panel.tsx` ‚Äî `WindowPanel` (exported as both `WindowPanel` and deprecated `StatusPanel`); wraps the identity rows (`tmx`, `cwd`, `git`) plus the **four orthogonal signal registers** (`out`/`agt`/`fab`/`PR` ‚Äî L0/L1/L2/L3, 3-char prefix vocabulary) in a `CollapsiblePanel` with copyable row interactions (via the file-private `CopyableRow`). Rewritten to the register view by `260706-y1ar` (the former mixed `run`/`agt` lines are gone; see ¬ß Pane panel four-register view). The `PR` (L3) register is **ungated from `fabChange`** ‚Äî shows for ANY pane with a derived `prNumber` (universal derivation); its interaction is **open-first** since `260703-41ks-pr-row-open-first-action` (the one row that isn't click-to-copy) ‚Äî with a PR URL the row body is a real anchor (file-private `PrLinkRow`) opening the PR in a new tab (always-visible inline `‚Üó`), and copy is role-swapped to a hover-revealed right-side icon (reusing the window-row icon-cluster gating); without a URL it stays a plain `CopyableRow` copying the segment text. See ¬ß PR Status. The panel's `headerRight` leads with a unified `<StatusDot win={win} />` before `{win.name}` ‚Äî an at-a-glance status summary that survives panel collapse; see ¬ß Status Dot
- `host-panel.tsx` ‚Äî `HostPanel`; hostname header + SSE dot inside a `CollapsiblePanel`, delegating the metric rows to the shared `HostMetrics` component (since `260701-vshd`; see ¬ß HostPanel). Keeps the `!metrics` "No metrics" branch
- `host-metrics.tsx` ‚Äî `HostMetrics`; the shared layout-agnostic presentational component rendering the CPU sparkline / memory gauge / disk+uptime / load rows for a `MetricsSnapshot` via `lib/sparkline.ts` + `lib/gauge.ts`. Consumed by both `HostPanel` (sidebar) and the `/` HOST HEALTH zone (`260701-vshd`; see ¬ß HostPanel)
- `server-panel.tsx` ‚Äî `ServerPanel`; swatch-style grid of server tiles (Mock A) inside a `CollapsiblePanel` with `title="Server"`, `storageKey="runkit-panel-server"`, `defaultOpen={false}`, `resizable={true}`, `defaultHeight={140}`, `minHeight={80}`, `mobileHeight={56}`. The active server name is rendered in the panel's `headerRight` slot with `truncate text-text-primary font-mono` (matching the WindowPanel/HostPanel header-right convention); the `LogoSpinner` follows the name when `refreshing` is true. The panel also passes `tint={activeTint}` + `tintOnlyWhenCollapsed` so the collapsed header background matches the selected server's `rowTints.get(activeColor).selected` shade (same body tint used by the active tile inside the panel) ‚Äî collapsed and expanded readings agree, and the header hover stays flat at the selected shade. Desktop grid: `repeat(auto-fill, minmax(72px, 1fr))`, 6px gap ‚Äî tiles expand to fill the sidebar width, multi-row, scrolls internally when overflowing the user-set height. Each tile is a focusable `<button role="option">` with a 4px top color stripe (ANSI tint via `rowTints.get(color).base`, neutral `--color-border` for tiles without an assigned color), 11px truncated name, 10px `{N} sess` meta. Active tile: `aria-current="true"` + inset accent ring + `rowTints.get(color).selected` body tint (accent-subtle fallback for untinted active server). Hover-revealed `.actions` cluster (color-picker `‚ñÝ` + kill `‚úï`) rendered as a sibling to the tile button (not nested ‚Äî avoids invalid button-in-button) with `group-hover:flex` on the outer wrapper; the cluster is shown on **every** tile (the color/kill affordances gate on `onColorClick`/`onKill` being passed, and `ServerPanel` passes `onKill` to every tile unconditionally ‚Äî `server-panel.tsx:165` ‚Äî not just the active one), and the entire cluster is hidden on `pointer: coarse`. Mobile layout (`@media (pointer: coarse), (max-width: 639px)`): single-row grid via `grid-auto-flow: column`, `grid-auto-columns: 88px`, `overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: hidden`, `scroll-snap-type: x mandatory` ‚Äî swipe horizontally, tap to select.
